export interface CanvasRef extends FC<CanvasProps> {
  makeImageSnapshot(rect?: SkRect): SkImage;
  makeImageSnapshotAsync(rect?: SkRect): Promise<SkImage>;
  redraw(): void;
  getNativeId(): number;
  measure(callback: MeasureOnSuccessCallback): void;
  measureInWindow(callback: MeasureInWindowOnSuccessCallback): void;
}

export const useCanvasRef = () => useRef<CanvasRef>(null);

const useReanimatedFrame = !HAS_REANIMATED_3 ? () => {} : Rea.useFrameCallback;
const measure = !HAS_REANIMATED_3 ? null : Rea.measure;

const useCanvasRefPriv: typeof useRef<View> = !HAS_REANIMATED_3
  ? useRef
  : Rea.useAnimatedRef;

export const useCanvasSize = (userRef?: RefObject<CanvasRef | null>) => {
  const ourRef = useCanvasRef();
  const ref = userRef ?? ourRef;
  const [size, setSize] = useState<SkSize>({ width: 0, height: 0 });
  useLayoutEffect(() => {
    if (ref.current) {
      ref.current.measure((_x, _y, width, height) => {
        setSize({ width, height });
      });
    }
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, []);
  return { ref, size };
};

  __destroyWebGLContextAfterRender?: boolean;
}

import type { SkCanvas } from "../Canvas";
import type { SkJSIInstance } from "../JsiInstance";
import type { SkRect } from "../Rect";

import type { SkPicture } from "./Picture";

export interface SkPictureRecorder extends SkJSIInstance<"PictureRecorder"> {
  /**
   * Returns a canvas on which to draw. When done drawing, call finishRecordingAsPicture()
   *
   * @param bounds - a rect to cull the results.
   */
  beginRecording(bounds?: SkRect): SkCanvas;

  /**
   * Returns the captured draw commands as a picture and invalidates the canvas returned earlier.
   */
  finishRecordingAsPicture(): SkPicture;
}

```
// ─── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
type RNSKPaint = ReturnType<typeof Skia.Paint>;

function makePaint(color: string, stroke = false, strokeWidth = 2): RNSKPaint {
  const p = Skia.Paint();
  p.setColor(Skia.Color(color));
  if (stroke) {
    p.setStyle(1); // stroke
    p.setStrokeWidth(strokeWidth);
  }
  return p;
}

// ─── Map renderer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const grassPath = (() => {
  const p = Skia.Path.Make();
  p.addRect(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, 1600, 1200));
  return p;
})();

function drawDecoration(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>,
  type: string,
  x: number,
  y: number,
  scale: number,
) {
  if (type === 'tree') {
    const s = scale;
    // Shadow
    const shadowPaint = makePaint(TREE_SHADOW);
    canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(x - 28 * s, y - 10 * s, 56 * s, 22 * s), shadowPaint);
    // Trunk
    const trunkPaint = makePaint(TREE_TRUNK);
    canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x - 7 * s, y - 20 * s, 14 * s, 36 * s), trunkPaint);
    // Crown layers
    const c1 = makePaint(TREE_CROWN1);
    const c2 = makePaint(TREE_CROWN2);
    canvas.drawCircle(x, y - 44 * s, 32 * s, c1);
    canvas.drawCircle(x - 18 * s, y - 30 * s, 24 * s, c1);
    canvas.drawCircle(x + 18 * s, y - 30 * s, 24 * s, c1);
    canvas.drawCircle(x, y - 54 * s, 22 * s, c2);
  } else if (type === 'bush') {
    const s = scale;
    const bd = makePaint(BUSH_DARK);
    const bb = makePaint(BUSH_BASE);
    const bh = makePaint(BUSH_HIGH);
    // Shadow
    canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(x - 26 * s, y - 8 * s, 52 * s, 18 * s), makePaint(TREE_SHADOW));
    canvas.drawCircle(x - 14 * s, y, 18 * s, bd);
    canvas.drawCircle(x + 14 * s, y, 18 * s, bd);
    canvas.drawCircle(x, y - 6 * s, 22 * s, bb);
    canvas.drawCircle(x - 14 * s, y - 2 * s, 16 * s, bb);
    canvas.drawCircle(x + 14 * s, y - 2 * s, 16 * s, bb);
    canvas.drawCircle(x, y - 12 * s, 14 * s, bh);
  } else if (type === 'ladder') {
    const lc = makePaint(LADDER_COLOR, true, 5);
    const lr = makePaint(LADDER_RUNG, true, 4);
    canvas.drawLine(x - 12, y - 40, x - 12, y + 40, lc);
    canvas.drawLine(x + 12, y - 40, x + 12, y + 40, lc);
    for (let i = -3; i <= 3; i++) {
      canvas.drawLine(x - 10, y + i * 13, x + 10, y + i * 13, lr);
    }
  }
}

function drawWall(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>,
  x: number, y: number, w: number, h: number,
) {
  // Shadow
  const shadow = makePaint(SHADOW_COLOR);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x + 6, y + 6, w, h), shadow);
  // Main face
  const main = makePaint(WALL_COLOR);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x, y, w, h), main);
  // Top highlight
  const top = makePaint(WALL_TOP);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x, y, w, 10), top);
  // Brick pattern (horizontal lines)
  const shade = makePaint(WALL_SHADE, true, 1.5);
  const lineCount = Math.floor(h / 20);
  for (let i = 1; i <= lineCount; i++) {
    canvas.drawLine(x, y + i * 20, x + w, y + i * 20, shade);
  }
  // Vertical brick offsets
  const brickCount = Math.floor(h / 20);
  for (let i = 0; i < brickCount; i++) {
    const offset = i % 2 === 0 ? w / 4 : w * 3 / 4;
    canvas.drawLine(x + offset, y + i * 20, x + offset, y + (i + 1) * 20, shade);
  }
}

function drawCrate(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>,
  x: number, y: number, w: number, h: number,
) {
  // Shadow
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x + 5, y + 5, w, h), makePaint(SHADOW_COLOR));
  // Base
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x, y, w, h), makePaint(CRATE_COLOR));
  // Light top
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x, y, w, 12), makePaint(CRATE_LIGHT));
  // Wood grain
  const grain = makePaint(CRATE_GRAIN, true, 2);
  canvas.drawLine(x + w * 0.25, y, x + w * 0.25, y + h, grain);
  canvas.drawLine(x + w * 0.75, y, x + w * 0.75, y + h, grain);
  canvas.drawLine(x, y + h * 0.5, x + w, y + h * 0.5, grain);
  // Border
  const border = makePaint(CRATE_GRAIN, true, 2.5);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x, y, w, h), border);
  // Corner nails
  const nail = makePaint('#FFE080');
  [[x + 6, y + 6], [x + w - 6, y + 6], [x + 6, y + h - 6], [x + w - 6, y + h - 6]].forEach(
    ([nx, ny]) => canvas.drawCircle(nx, ny, 3, nail),
  );
}

/** Draw the entire static map (ground + walls + crates + decorations) */
export function drawMap(canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>) {
  'worklet';
  // Ground
  const lightGrass = makePaint(GRASS_LIGHT);
  canvas.drawPath(grassPath, lightGrass);

  // Grass tile checkerboard
  const darkGrass = makePaint(GRASS_DARK);
  const tileSize = 80;
  for (let gy = 0; gy < 1200; gy += tileSize) {
    for (let gx = 0; gx < 1600; gx += tileSize) {
      if ((Math.floor(gx / tileSize) + Math.floor(gy / tileSize)) % 2 === 1) {
        canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(gx, gy, tileSize, tileSize), darkGrass);
      }
    }
  }

  // Decorations (behind walls)
  for (let i = 0; i < MAP_DECORATIONS.length; i++) {
    const d = MAP_DECORATIONS[i];
    drawDecoration(canvas, d.type, d.x, d.y, d.scale ?? 1);
  }

  // Walls & crates
  for (let i = 0; i < MAP_TILES.length; i++) {
    const t = MAP_TILES[i];
    const { x, y, w, h } = t.rect;
    if (t.type === 'wall') drawWall(canvas, x, y, w, h);
    else drawCrate(canvas, x, y, w, h);
  }
}

// ─── Player renderer ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/** Compute animation frame index */
function getAnimFrame(
  animState: string,
  animClock: number,
): number {
  'worklet';
  if (animState === 'running') {
    return Math.floor(animClock / RUN_FRAME_DURATION) % RUN_FRAMES;
  }
  return Math.floor(animClock / IDLE_FRAME_DURATION) % IDLE_FRAMES;
}

/** Draw the cute cartoon character */
export function drawPlayer(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>,
  px: number,
  py: number,
  facing: string,
  animState: string,
  animClock: number,
  hasBomb: boolean,
) {
  'worklet';
  const frame = getAnimFrame(animState, animClock);
  const isRunning = animState === 'running';
  const flip = facing === 'left' ? -1 : 1;

  // Bob offset for running
  const bobY = isRunning ? (frame % 2 === 0 ? -3 : 2) : (frame === 0 ? 0 : -2);

  canvas.save();
  canvas.translate(px, py + bobY);
  canvas.scale(flip, 1);

  // Shadow
  canvas.drawOval(
    Skia.XYWHRect(-18, PLAYER_HALF - 4, 36, 12),
    makePaint('rgba(0,0,0,0.25)'),
  );

  // Shoes
  const shoePaint = makePaint(PLAYER_SHOE);
  const shoeOffsetL = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? -4 : 4) : 0;
  const shoeOffsetR = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? 4 : -4) : 0;
  canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(-18 + shoeOffsetL, PLAYER_HALF - 8, 14, 10), shoePaint);
  canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(5 + shoeOffsetR, PLAYER_HALF - 8, 14, 10), shoePaint);

  // Legs
  const legPaint = makePaint(PLAYER_OVERALLS);
  const legOffsetL = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? -3 : 3) : 0;
  const legOffsetR = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? 3 : -3) : 0;
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(-14, PLAYER_HALF - 22 + legOffsetL, 10, 18), legPaint);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(4, PLAYER_HALF - 22 + legOffsetR, 10, 18), legPaint);

  // Body (overalls)
  const bodyPaint = makePaint(PLAYER_BODY);
  canvas.drawRRect(
    Skia.RRectXY(Skia.XYWHRect(-16, -18, 32, 30), 8, 8),
    bodyPaint,
  );
  const overallsPaint = makePaint(PLAYER_OVERALLS);
  canvas.drawRRect(
    Skia.RRectXY(Skia.XYWHRect(-12, -6, 24, 20), 4, 4),
    overallsPaint,
  );

  // Arms
  const armPaint = makePaint(PLAYER_BODY);
  const armSwingL = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? 8 : -8) : 0;
  const armSwingR = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? -8 : 8) : 0;
  // Left arm
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(-26, -14 + armSwingL, 12, 8), armPaint);
  // Right arm
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(14, -14 + armSwingR, 12, 8), armPaint);

  // Bomb in right hand
  if (hasBomb) {
    drawBombOnHand(canvas, 26, -14 + armSwingR);
  }

  // Head
  const skinPaint = makePaint(PLAYER_SKIN);
  const idleBob = !isRunning && frame === 1 ? -1 : 0;
  canvas.drawCircle(0, -30 + idleBob, 18, skinPaint);

  // Hat
  const hatPaint = makePaint(PLAYER_HAT);
  const hatBrimPaint = makePaint('#3A80CC');
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(-14, -50 + idleBob, 28, 6), hatBrimPaint);
  canvas.drawRRect(
    Skia.RRectXY(Skia.XYWHRect(-10, -66 + idleBob, 20, 18), 4, 4),
    hatPaint,
  );

  // Eyes
  const eyePaint = makePaint(PLAYER_EYE);
  const eyeWhitePaint = makePaint('#FFFFFF');
  canvas.drawCircle(-7, -32 + idleBob, 5, eyeWhitePaint);
  canvas.drawCircle(7, -32 + idleBob, 5, eyeWhitePaint);
  canvas.drawCircle(-6, -31 + idleBob, 3, eyePaint);
  canvas.drawCircle(8, -31 + idleBob, 3, eyePaint);
  // Eye shine
  const shinePaint = makePaint('#FFFFFF');
  canvas.drawCircle(-5, -33 + idleBob, 1.2, shinePaint);
  canvas.drawCircle(9, -33 + idleBob, 1.2, shinePaint);

  // Mouth (smile)
  const mouthPath = Skia.Path.Make();
  mouthPath.moveTo(-5, -24 + idleBob);
  mouthPath.quadTo(0, -20 + idleBob, 5, -24 + idleBob);
  const mouthPaint = makePaint(PLAYER_MOUTH, true, 2);
  canvas.drawPath(mouthPath, mouthPaint);

  // Cheeks
  const cheekPaint = makePaint('rgba(255,150,150,0.5)');
  canvas.drawCircle(-10, -27 + idleBob, 4, cheekPaint);
  canvas.drawCircle(10, -27 + idleBob, 4, cheekPaint);

  canvas.restore();
}

function drawBombOnHand(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>,
  hx: number, hy: number,
) {
  'worklet';
  const r = 9;
  // Bomb body
  canvas.drawCircle(hx, hy, r, makePaint(BOMB_BODY));
  // Wick
  const wickPath = Skia.Path.Make();
  wickPath.moveTo(hx, hy - r);
  wickPath.quadTo(hx + 8, hy - r - 10, hx + 4, hy - r - 18);
  canvas.drawPath(wickPath, makePaint(BOMB_WICK, true, 2.5));
  // Spark
  canvas.drawCircle(hx + 4, hy - r - 18, 3, makePaint('#FFDD00'));
  // Shine
  canvas.drawCircle(hx - 3, hy - 3, 2.5, makePaint(BOMB_SHINE));
}

// ─── Bomb renderer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export function drawBomb(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>,
  bomb: BombState,
  playerX: number,
  playerY: number,
  timeSec: number,
) {
  'worklet';
  if (bomb.pickedUp && !bomb.exploded) return; // drawn on player's hand
  if (bomb.exploded) {
    drawExplosion(canvas, playerX, playerY, bomb.explosionTime);
    return;
  }

  const { x, y } = bomb;
  const r = BOMB_SIZE / 2;

  // Shadow
  canvas.drawOval(
    Skia.XYWHRect(x - r - 4, y + r - 6, (r + 4) * 2, 12),
    makePaint(SHADOW_COLOR),
  );

  // Pulse scale based on countdown
  const urgency = Math.max(0, 1 - (bomb.countdown / 20));
  const pulse = 1 + urgency * 0.15 * Math.sin(timeSec * 10);

  canvas.save();
  canvas.translate(x, y);
  canvas.scale(pulse, pulse);

  // Body
  canvas.drawCircle(0, 0, r, makePaint(BOMB_BODY));
  // Highlight ring
  canvas.drawCircle(0, 0, r, makePaint('rgba(255,255,255,0.08)', true, 2));
  // Shine
  canvas.drawCircle(-r * 0.3, -r * 0.3, r * 0.25, makePaint(BOMB_SHINE));
  // Wick
  const wickPath = Skia.Path.Make();
  wickPath.moveTo(0, -r);
  wickPath.quadTo(10, -r - 14, 5, -r - 24);
  canvas.drawPath(wickPath, makePaint(BOMB_WICK, true, 3));
  // Spark (blinks faster near explosion)
  const blinkRate = 6 + urgency * 20;
  if (Math.sin(timeSec * blinkRate) > 0) {
    canvas.drawCircle(5, -r - 24, 4, makePaint('#FFDD00'));
    canvas.drawCircle(5, -r - 24, 2, makePaint('#FFFFFF'));
  }

  canvas.restore();
}

function drawExplosion(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.Canvas>,
  x: number, y: number, elapsed: number,
) {
  'worklet';
  const t = Math.min(elapsed / EXPLOSION_DURATION, 1);
  if (t >= 1) return;

  const expandT = t < 0.4 ? t / 0.4 : 1;
  const fadeT = t > 0.5 ? (t - 0.5) / 0.5 : 0;
  const alpha = 1 - fadeT;
  const r = EXPLOSION_RADIUS * expandT;

  // Outer glow
  const outerPaint = Skia.Paint();
  outerPaint.setColor(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,80,0,${0.4 * alpha})`));
  canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 1.8, outerPaint);

  // Mid ring
  const midPaint = Skia.Paint();
  midPaint.setColor(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,136,0,${0.7 * alpha})`));
  canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 1.2, midPaint);

  // Core
  const corePaint = Skia.Paint();
  corePaint.setColor(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,238,68,${alpha})`));
  canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 0.7, corePaint);

  // White flash at start
  if (t < 0.15) {
    const flashAlpha = 1 - t / 0.15;
    const flashPaint = Skia.Paint();
    flashPaint.setColor(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,255,255,${flashAlpha * 0.9})`));
    canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 0.5, flashPaint);
  }

  // Flying debris lines
  const debrisCount = 8;
  for (let i = 0; i < debrisCount; i++) {
    const angle = (i / debrisCount) * Math.PI * 2;
    const len = r * (0.6 + (i % 3) * 0.2);
    const dx = Math.cos(angle);
    const dy = Math.sin(angle);
    const debrisPaint = makePaint(`rgba(255,200,0,${alpha * 0.8})`, true, 3);
    canvas.drawLine(
      x + dx * r * 0.3,
      y + dy * r * 0.3,
      x + dx * len,
      y + dy * len,
      debrisPaint,
    );
  }
}
```

```
// ─── Paint factory (worklet-safe) ─────────────────────────────────────────────
type SkiaCanvas = ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder>['beginRecording'];

function mp(color: string, stroke = false, sw = 2) {
  'worklet';
  const p = Skia.Paint();
  p.setColor(Skia.Color(color));
  if (stroke) { p.setStyle(1); p.setStrokeWidth(sw); }
  return p;
}

// ─── Decoration drawing ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function drawDecoration(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
  type: string, x: number, y: number, scale: number,
) {

    canvas.drawCircle(x,        y - 44*s, 32*s, mp(TREE_CROWN1));
    canvas.drawCircle(x - 18*s, y - 30*s, 24*s, mp(TREE_CROWN1));
    canvas.drawCircle(x + 18*s, y - 30*s, 24*s, mp(TREE_CROWN1));
    canvas.drawCircle(x,        y - 54*s, 22*s, mp(TREE_CROWN2));
  } else if (type === 'bush') {
    canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(x - 26*s, y - 8*s, 52*s, 18*s), mp(TREE_SHADOW));
    canvas.drawCircle(x - 14*s, y,       18*s, mp(BUSH_DARK));
    canvas.drawCircle(x + 14*s, y,       18*s, mp(BUSH_DARK));
    canvas.drawCircle(x,        y -  6*s, 22*s, mp(BUSH_BASE));
    canvas.drawCircle(x - 14*s, y -  2*s, 16*s, mp(BUSH_BASE));
    canvas.drawCircle(x + 14*s, y -  2*s, 16*s, mp(BUSH_BASE));
    canvas.drawCircle(x,        y - 12*s, 14*s, mp(BUSH_HIGH));
  } else if (type === 'ladder') {
    const lc = mp(LADDER_COLOR, true, 5);
    const lr = mp(LADDER_RUNG,  true, 4);
    canvas.drawLine(x - 12, y - 40, x - 12, y + 40, lc);

    for (let i = -3; i <= 3; i++) {
      canvas.drawLine(x - 10, y + i*13, x + 10, y + i*13, lr);
    }
  }
}

function drawWall(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
  x: number, y: number, w: number, h: number,
) {

  }

function drawCrate(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
  x: number, y: number, w: number, h: number,
) {
  'worklet';
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x+5, y+5, w, h), mp(SHADOW_COLOR));
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x,   y,   w, h), mp(CRATE_COLOR));

  const grain = mp(CRATE_GRAIN, true, 2);
  canvas.drawLine(x+w*0.25, y, x+w*0.25, y+h, grain);
  canvas.drawLine(x+w*0.75, y, x+w*0.75, y+h, grain);
  canvas.drawLine(x, y+h*0.5, x+w, y+h*0.5, grain);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(x, y, w, h), mp(CRATE_GRAIN, true, 2.5));
  const nail = mp('#FFE080');
  canvas.drawCircle(x+6,   y+6,   3, nail);
  canvas.drawCircle(x+w-6, y+6,   3, nail);
  canvas.drawCircle(x+6,   y+h-6, 3, nail);
  canvas.drawCircle(x+w-6, y+h-6, 3, nail);
}

// ─── Map renderer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export function drawMap(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
) {
  'worklet';
  // Ground fill
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, 1600, 1200), mp(GRASS_LIGHT));
  // Checkerboard tiles
  const ts = 80;
  const dark = mp(GRASS_DARK);
  for (let gy = 0; gy < 1200; gy += ts) {
    for (let gx = 0; gx < 1600; gx += ts) {
      if (((gx/ts) + (gy/ts)) % 2 === 1) {
        canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(gx, gy, ts, ts), dark);
      }
    }
  }
  // Decorations
  for (let i = 0; i < MAP_DECORATIONS.length; i++) {
    const d = MAP_DECORATIONS[i];
    drawDecoration(canvas, d.type, d.x, d.y, d.scale ?? 1);
  }
  // Tiles (walls + crates)
  for (let i = 0; i < MAP_TILES.length; i++) {
    const t = MAP_TILES[i];
    const { x, y, w, h } = t.rect;
    if (t.type === 'wall') drawWall(canvas, x, y, w, h);
    else drawCrate(canvas, x, y, w, h);
  }
}

// ─── Player renderer ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function getAnimFrame(animState: string, animClock: number): number {
  'worklet';
  if (animState === 'running') return Math.floor(animClock / RUN_FRAME_DURATION) % RUN_FRAMES;
  return Math.floor(animClock / IDLE_FRAME_DURATION) % IDLE_FRAMES;
}

export function drawPlayer(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
  px: number, py: number,
  facing: string, animState: string, animClock: number, hasBomb: boolean,
) {
  'worklet';
  const frame = getAnimFrame(animState, animClock);
  const isRunning = animState === 'running';
  const flip = facing === 'left' ? -1 : 1;
  const bobY = isRunning ? (frame % 2 === 0 ? -3 : 2) : (frame === 0 ? 0 : -2);

  canvas.save();
  canvas.translate(px, py + bobY);
  canvas.scale(flip, 1);

  // Shadow
  canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(-18, PLAYER_HALF-4, 36, 12), mp('rgba(0,0,0,0.25)'));

  // Shoes
  const shoe = mp(PLAYER_SHOE);
  const sL = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? -4 :  4) : 0;
  const sR = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ?  4 : -4) : 0;
  canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(-18+sL, PLAYER_HALF-8, 14, 10), shoe);
  canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(  5+sR, PLAYER_HALF-8, 14, 10), shoe);

  // Legs
  const leg = mp(PLAYER_OVERALLS);
  const lL = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? -3 :  3) : 0;
  const lR = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ?  3 : -3) : 0;
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(-14, PLAYER_HALF-22+lL, 10, 18), leg);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(  4, PLAYER_HALF-22+lR, 10, 18), leg);

  // Body
  canvas.drawRRect(Skia.RRectXY(Skia.XYWHRect(-16, -18, 32, 30), 8, 8), mp(PLAYER_BODY));
  canvas.drawRRect(Skia.RRectXY(Skia.XYWHRect(-12,  -6, 24, 20), 4, 4), mp(PLAYER_OVERALLS));

  // Arms
  const arm = mp(PLAYER_BODY);
  const aL = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ?  8 : -8) : 0;
  const aR = isRunning ? (frame < 2 ? -8 :  8) : 0;
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(-26, -14+aL, 12, 8), arm);
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect( 14, -14+aR, 12, 8), arm);

  // Bomb in hand
  if (hasBomb) {
    drawBombOnHand(canvas, 26, -14+aR);
  }

  // Head
  const idleBob = !isRunning && frame === 1 ? -1 : 0;
  canvas.drawCircle(0, -30+idleBob, 18, mp(PLAYER_SKIN));

  // Hat brim + crown
  canvas.drawRect(Skia.XYWHRect(-14, -50+idleBob, 28, 6), mp(PLAYER_HAT2));
  canvas.drawRRect(Skia.RRectXY(Skia.XYWHRect(-10, -66+idleBob, 20, 18), 4, 4), mp(PLAYER_HAT));

  // Eyes
  const ew = mp('#FFFFFF');
  const eb = mp(PLAYER_EYE);
  canvas.drawCircle(-7, -32+idleBob, 5, ew);
  canvas.drawCircle( 7, -32+idleBob, 5, ew);
  canvas.drawCircle(-6, -31+idleBob, 3, eb);
  canvas.drawCircle( 8, -31+idleBob, 3, eb);
  canvas.drawCircle(-5, -33+idleBob, 1.2, mp('#FFFFFF'));
  canvas.drawCircle( 9, -33+idleBob, 1.2, mp('#FFFFFF'));

  // Smile
  const mouth = Skia.Path.Make();
  mouth.moveTo(-5, -24+idleBob);
  mouth.quadTo(0, -20+idleBob, 5, -24+idleBob);
  canvas.drawPath(mouth, mp(PLAYER_MOUTH, true, 2));

  // Cheeks
  canvas.drawCircle(-10, -27+idleBob, 4, mp('rgba(255,150,150,0.5)'));
  canvas.drawCircle( 10, -27+idleBob, 4, mp('rgba(255,150,150,0.5)'));

  canvas.restore();
}

function drawBombOnHand(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
  hx: number, hy: number,
) {
  'worklet';
  const r = 9;
  canvas.drawCircle(hx, hy, r, mp(BOMB_BODY_C));
  const w = Skia.Path.Make();
  w.moveTo(hx, hy - r);
  w.quadTo(hx+8, hy-r-10, hx+4, hy-r-18);
  canvas.drawPath(w, mp(BOMB_WICK_C, true, 2.5));
  canvas.drawCircle(hx+4, hy-r-18, 3, mp('#FFDD00'));
  canvas.drawCircle(hx-3, hy-3, 2.5, mp('rgba(255,255,255,0.3)'));
}

// ─── Bomb renderer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export function drawBomb(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
  bomb: BombState,
  playerX: number, playerY: number,
  timeSec: number,
) {
  'worklet';
  if (bomb.pickedUp && !bomb.exploded) return;
  if (bomb.exploded) {
    drawExplosion(canvas, playerX, playerY, bomb.explosionTime);
    return;
  }

  const { x, y } = bomb;
  const r = BOMB_SIZE / 2;

  canvas.drawOval(Skia.XYWHRect(x-r-4, y+r-6, (r+4)*2, 12), mp(SHADOW_COLOR));

  const urgency = Math.max(0, 1 - (bomb.countdown / 20));
  const pulse = 1 + urgency * 0.15 * Math.sin(timeSec * 10);

  canvas.save();
  canvas.translate(x, y);
  canvas.scale(pulse, pulse);

  canvas.drawCircle(0, 0, r, mp(BOMB_BODY_C));
  canvas.drawCircle(0, 0, r, mp('rgba(255,255,255,0.08)', true, 2));
  canvas.drawCircle(-r*0.3, -r*0.3, r*0.25, mp('rgba(255,255,255,0.3)'));

  const wick = Skia.Path.Make();
  wick.moveTo(0, -r);
  wick.quadTo(10, -r-14, 5, -r-24);
  canvas.drawPath(wick, mp(BOMB_WICK_C, true, 3));

  const blinkRate = 6 + urgency * 20;
  if (Math.sin(timeSec * blinkRate) > 0) {
    canvas.drawCircle(5, -r-24, 4, mp('#FFDD00'));
    canvas.drawCircle(5, -r-24, 2, mp('#FFFFFF'));
  }

  canvas.restore();
}

function drawExplosion(
  canvas: ReturnType<typeof Skia.PictureRecorder.prototype.beginRecording>,
  x: number, y: number, elapsed: number,
) {
  'worklet';
  const t = Math.min(elapsed / EXPLOSION_DURATION, 1);
  if (t >= 1) return;

  const expandT = t < 0.4 ? t / 0.4 : 1;
  const fadeT = t > 0.5 ? (t - 0.5) / 0.5 : 0;
  const alpha = 1 - fadeT;
  const r = EXPLOSION_RADIUS * expandT;

  const outer = Skia.Paint();
  outer.setColor(Skia.Color(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,80,0,${(0.4 * alpha).toFixed(3)})`)));
  canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 1.8, outer);

  const mid = Skia.Paint();
  mid.setColor(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,136,0,${(0.7 * alpha).toFixed(3)})`));
  canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 1.2, mid);

  const core = Skia.Paint();
  core.setColor(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,238,68,${alpha.toFixed(3)})`));
  canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 0.7, core);

  if (t < 0.15) {
    const fA = 1 - t / 0.15;
    const flash = Skia.Paint();
    flash.setColor(Skia.Color(`rgba(255,255,255,${(fA * 0.9).toFixed(3)})`));
    canvas.drawCircle(x, y, r * 0.5, flash);
  }

  const debris = mp(`rgba(255,200,0,${(alpha * 0.8).toFixed(3)})`, true, 3);
  for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
    const angle = (i / 8) * Math.PI * 2;
    const len = r * (0.6 + (i % 3) * 0.2);
    const dx = Math.cos(angle);
    const dy = Math.sin(angle);
    canvas.drawLine(x+dx*r*0.3, y+dy*r*0.3, x+dx*len, y+dy*len, debris);
  }
}
```

```
export default function GameCanvas({
  screenW,
  screenH,
  joystickX,
  joystickY,
  isPaused,
  onFpsUpdate,
  onTimerUpdate,
  onBombPickup,
  onGameOver,
}: GameCanvasProps) {
  const canvasRef = useCanvasRef();

  // Game state lives in a ref so it's accessible from the frame callback
  const gameStateRef = useRef<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);

  // Shared values for inter-thread communication
  const fpsShared = useSharedValue(60);
  const timerShared = useSharedValue(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
  const bombPickedShared = useSharedValue(false);
  const gameOverShared = useSharedValue(false);

  // JS-thread polling for UI updates
  const lastFpsRef = useRef(60);
  const lastTimerRef = useRef(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
  const lastBombPickedRef = useRef(false);
  const lastGameOverRef = useRef(false);

  // Running time for spark animation
  const elapsedRef = useSharedValue(0);

  // ── Frame callback — runs on UI thread at 60 fps ────────────────────────────
  useFrameCallback((info) => {
    'worklet';
    const dtMs = info.timeSincePreviousFrame ?? 16;
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;

    elapsedRef.value += dtMs / 1000;

    // Merge pause from JS thread
    const state = gameStateRef.value as GameState;
    const stateWithPause = { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value };

    // Tick game logic
    const next = gameTick(
      stateWithPause,
      joystickX.value,
      joystickY.value,
      screenW,
      screenH,
      dtMs,
    );

    // Update hasBomb flag
    if (next.bomb.pickedUp && !next.player.hasBomb) {
      (next.player as any).hasBomb = true;
    }
    if (next.player.hasBomb !== next.bomb.pickedUp) {
      next.player.hasBomb = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    }

    gameStateRef.value = next;

    // Push signals for JS-thread UI
    fpsShared.value = next.fps;
    timerShared.value = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
    bombPickedShared.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    gameOverShared.value = next.isGameOver;

    // ── Draw frame ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const cam = next.camera;
    const shakeX = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? (Math.random() - 0.5) * cam.shakeIntensity
      : 0;
    const shakeY = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? (Math.random() - 0.5) * cam.shakeIntensity
      : 0;

    canvas.clear(Skia.Color('#7EC850'));
    canvas.save();
    canvas.translate(
      -(cam.x + shakeX),
      -(cam.y + shakeY),
    );

    drawMap(canvas);

    drawBomb(
      canvas,
      next.bomb,
      next.player.x,
      next.player.y,
      elapsedRef.value,
    );

    drawPlayer(
      canvas,
      next.player.x,
      next.player.y,
      next.player.facing,
      next.player.animState,
      next.player.animClock,
      next.player.hasBomb,
    );

    canvas.restore();
  });

  // ── JS-thread polling loop for UI callbacks ─────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    let rafId: number;
    const poll = () => {
      const fps = fpsShared.value;
      const timer = timerShared.value;
      const picked = bombPickedShared.value;
      const over = gameOverShared.value;

      if (fps !== lastFpsRef.current) {
        lastFpsRef.current = fps;
        onFpsUpdate(fps);
      }
      if (timer !== lastTimerRef.current) {
        lastTimerRef.current = timer;
        onTimerUpdate(timer);
      }
      if (picked && !lastBombPickedRef.current) {
        lastBombPickedRef.current = true;
        onBombPickup();
      }
      if (over && !lastGameOverRef.current) {
        lastGameOverRef.current = true;
        onGameOver();
      }
      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    };
    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
  }, [fpsShared, timerShared, bombPickedShared, gameOverShared, onFpsUpdate, onTimerUpdate, onBombPickup, onGameOver]);

  return (
    <Canvas
      ref={canvasRef}
      style={StyleSheet.absoluteFill}
    />
  );
}
```

```
import React, { useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { Canvas, Picture, Skia } from '@shopify/react-native-skia';
import { StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import { useFrameCallback, useSharedValue } from 'react-native-reanimated';
import type { SkPicture } from '@shopify/react-native-skia';

import { BOMB_COUNTDOWN, BOMB_SPAWN, PLAYER_SPAWN } from '../../game/constants';
import { gameTick } from '../../game/gameLogic';
import type { GameState } from '../../game/types';
import { drawBomb, drawMap, drawPlayer } from './renderers';

interface GameCanvasProps {
  screenW: number;
  screenH: number;
  joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  isPaused: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<boolean>>;
  onFpsUpdate: (fps: number) => void;
  onTimerUpdate: (seconds: number) => void;
  onBombPickup: () => void;
  onGameOver: () => void;
}

const INITIAL_STATE: GameState = {
  player: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y,
    vx: 0,
    vy: 0,
    facing: 'right',
    animState: 'idle',
    animClock: 0,
    hasBomb: false,
  },
  camera: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x - 400,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y - 300,
    shakeIntensity: 0,
    shakeDuration: 0,
    shakeElapsed: 0,
  },
  bomb: {
    x: BOMB_SPAWN.x,
    y: BOMB_SPAWN.y,
    pickedUp: false,
    countdown: BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
    exploded: false,
    explosionTime: 0,
  },
  isPaused: false,
  isGameOver: false,
  fps: 60,
  fpsAccumulator: 0,
  fpsFrameCount: 0,
};

// Empty placeholder picture until the first frame is drawn
function makeEmptyPicture(): SkPicture {
  const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
  rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, 1, 1));
  return rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
}

export default function GameCanvas({
  screenW,
  screenH,
  joystickX,
  joystickY,
  isPaused,
  onFpsUpdate,
  onTimerUpdate,
  onBombPickup,
  onGameOver,
}: GameCanvasProps) {
  // The rendered scene, updated every frame on the UI thread
  const scenePicture = useSharedValue<SkPicture>(makeEmptyPicture());

  // Full game state lives as a shared value so it's accessible from the UI-thread worklet
  const gameState = useSharedValue<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);

  // Running time (seconds) for spark/pulse animations
  const elapsed = useSharedValue(0);

  // UI-thread signals pushed back to JS thread for HUD display
  const fpsSignal       = useSharedValue(60);
  const timerSignal     = useSharedValue(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
  const bombPickSignal  = useSharedValue(false);
  const gameOverSignal  = useSharedValue(false);

  // ── Main game loop — UI thread, ~60 fps ──────────────────────────────────────
  useFrameCallback((info) => {
    'worklet';
    const dtMs = info.timeSincePreviousFrame ?? 16.67;
    elapsed.value += dtMs / 1000;

    // Tick game logic
    const state = gameState.value;
    const merged = { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value };
    const next = gameTick(merged, joystickX.value, joystickY.value, screenW, screenH, dtMs);
    gameState.value = next;

    // Push HUD signals
    fpsSignal.value      = next.fps;
    timerSignal.value    = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
    bombPickSignal.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    gameOverSignal.value = next.isGameOver;

    // ── Draw scene into a picture ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
    const cvs = rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, screenW, screenH));

    // Camera transform + shake
    const cam = next.camera;
    const shakeX = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? (Math.random() - 0.5) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;
    const shakeY = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? (Math.random() - 0.5) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;

    cvs.save();
    cvs.translate(-(cam.x + shakeX), -(cam.y + shakeY));

    drawMap(cvs);

    drawBomb(
      cvs,
      next.bomb,
      next.player.x,
      next.player.y,
      elapsed.value,
    );

    drawPlayer(
      cvs,
      next.player.x,
      next.player.y,
      next.player.facing,
      next.player.animState,
      next.player.animClock,
      next.player.hasBomb,
    );

    cvs.restore();

    scenePicture.value = rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
  });

  // ── JS-thread polling: sync shared value signals → React state callbacks ─────
  useEffect(() => {
    let rafId: number;
    let lastFps   = 60;
    let lastTimer = BOMB_COUNTDOWN;
    let lastPick  = false;
    let lastOver  = false;

    const poll = () => {
      const fps   = fpsSignal.value;
      const timer = timerSignal.value;
      const pick  = bombPickSignal.value;
      const over  = gameOverSignal.value;

      if (fps !== lastFps)     { lastFps   = fps;   onFpsUpdate(fps); }
      if (timer !== lastTimer) { lastTimer = timer; onTimerUpdate(timer); }
      if (pick  && !lastPick)  { lastPick  = true;  onBombPickup(); }
      if (over  && !lastOver)  { lastOver  = true;  onGameOver(); }

      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    };
    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
  }, [fpsSignal, timerSignal, bombPickSignal, gameOverSignal,
      onFpsUpdate, onTimerUpdate, onBombPickup, onGameOver]);

  return (
    <Canvas style={StyleSheet.absoluteFill}>
      <Picture picture={scenePicture} />
    </Canvas>
  );
}
```

     1 import React, { useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
     2 import { Skia } from '@shopify/react-native-skia';

     4 import {
     5   BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
     6   BOMB_SPAWN,
     7   PLAYER_SPAWN,
     8 } from '../../game/constants';
     9 import { gameTick } from '../../game/gameLogic';
    10 import type { GameState } from '../../game/types';
    11 import { drawBomb, drawMap, drawPlayer } from './renderers';
    12 
    13 interface GameCanvasProps {
    14   screenW: number;
    15   screenH: number;
    16   joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
    17   joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
    18   isPaused: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<boolean>>;
    19   onFpsUpdate: (fps: number) => void;
    20   onTimerUpdate: (seconds: number) => void;
    21   onBombPickup: () => void;
    22   onGameOver: () => void;
    23 }
    24 
    25 const INITIAL_STATE: GameState = {
    26   player: {
    27     x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x,
    28     y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y,
    29     vx: 0,
    30     vy: 0,
    31     facing: 'right',
    32     animState: 'idle',
    33     animClock: 0,
    34     hasBomb: false,
    35   },
    36   camera: {
    37     x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x - 400,
    38     y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y - 300,
    39     shakeIntensity: 0,
    40     shakeDuration: 0,
    41     shakeElapsed: 0,
    42   },
    43   bomb: {
    44     x: BOMB_SPAWN.x,
    45     y: BOMB_SPAWN.y,
    46     pickedUp: false,
    47     countdown: BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
    48     exploded: false,
    49     explosionTime: 0,
    50   },
    51   isPaused: false,
    52   isGameOver: false,
    53   fps: 60,
    54   fpsAccumulator: 0,
    55   fpsFrameCount: 0,
    56 };
    57 
    58 // Empty placeholder picture until the first frame is drawn
    59 function makeEmptyPicture(): SkPicture {
    60   const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
    61   rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, 1, 1));
    62   return rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
    63 }
    64 
    65 export default function GameCanvas({
    66   screenW,
    67   screenH,
    68   joystickX,
    69   joystickY,
    70   isPaused,
    71   onFpsUpdate,
    72   onTimerUpdate,
    73   onBombPickup,
    74   onGameOver,
    75 }: GameCanvasProps) {
    76   // The rendered scene, updated every frame on the UI thread
    77   const scenePicture = useSharedValue<SkPicture>(makeEmptyPicture());
    78 
    79   // Full game state lives as a shared value so it's accessible from the UI-thread worklet
    80   const gameState = useSharedValue<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);
    81 
    82   // Running time (seconds) for spark/pulse animations
    83   const elapsed = useSharedValue(0);
    84 
    85   // UI-thread signals pushed back to JS thread for HUD display
    86   const fpsSignal       = useSharedValue(60);
    87   const timerSignal     = useSharedValue(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
    88   const bombPickSignal  = useSharedValue(false);
    89   const gameOverSignal  = useSharedValue(false);
    90 
    91   // ── Main game loop — UI thread, ~60 fps ──────────────────────────────────────
    92   useFrameCallback((info) => {
    93     'worklet';
    94     const dtMs = info.timeSincePreviousFrame ?? 16.67;
    95     elapsed.value += dtMs / 1000;
    96 
    97     // Tick game logic
    98     const state = gameState.value;
    99     const merged = { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value };
   100     const next = gameTick(merged, joystickX.value, joystickY.value, screenW, screenH, dtMs);
   101     gameState.value = next;
   102 
   103     // Push HUD signals
   104     fpsSignal.value      = next.fps;
   105     timerSignal.value    = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
   106     bombPickSignal.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
   107     gameOverSignal.value = next.isGameOver;
   108 
   109     // ── Draw scene into a picture ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   110     const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
   111     const cvs = rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, screenW, screenH));
   112 
   113     // Camera transform + shake
   114     const cam = next.camera;
   115     const shakeX = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
   116       ? (Math.random() - 0.5) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;
   117     const shakeY = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
   118       ? (Math.random() - 0.5) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;
   119 
   120     cvs.save();
   121     cvs.translate(-(cam.x + shakeX), -(cam.y + shakeY));
   122 
   123     drawMap(cvs);
   124 
   125     drawBomb(
   126       cvs,
   127       next.bomb,
   128       next.player.x,
   129       next.player.y,
   130       elapsed.value,
   131     );
   132 
   133     drawPlayer(
   134       cvs,
   135       next.player.x,
   136       next.player.y,
   137       next.player.facing,
   138       next.player.animState,
   139       next.player.animClock,
   140       next.player.hasBomb,
   141     );
   142 
   143     cvs.restore();
   144 
   145     scenePicture.value = rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
   146   });
   147 
   148   // ── JS-thread polling: sync shared value signals → React state callbacks ─────
   149   useEffect(() => {
   150     let rafId: number;
   151     let lastFps   = 60;
   152     let lastTimer = BOMB_COUNTDOWN;
   153     let lastPick  = false;
   154     let lastOver  = false;
   155 
   156     const poll = () => {
   157       const fps   = fpsSignal.value;
   158       const timer = timerSignal.value;
   159       const pick  = bombPickSignal.value;
   160       const over  = gameOverSignal.value;
   161 
   162       if (fps !== lastFps)     { lastFps   = fps;   onFpsUpdate(fps); }
   163       if (timer !== lastTimer) { lastTimer = timer; onTimerUpdate(timer); }
   164       if (pick  && !lastPick)  { lastPick  = true;  onBombPickup(); }
   165       if (over  && !lastOver)  { lastOver  = true;  onGameOver(); }
   166 
   167       rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
   168     };
   169     rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
   170     return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
   171   }, [fpsSignal, timerSignal, bombPickSignal, gameOverSignal,
   172       onFpsUpdate, onTimerUpdate, onBombPickup, onGameOver]);
   173 
   174   return (
   175     <Canvas style={StyleSheet.absoluteFill}>
   176       <Picture picture={scenePicture} />
   177     </Canvas>
   178   );
   179 }

Application Overview\n\n**Application Name**: Premium 2D Party Game Prototype\n\n**Description**: A landscape-oriented mobile party game featuring a single playable character navigating a test arena. The player collects a bomb with a countdown timer, and the game ends when the timer reaches zero. This is the first playable prototype focusing on core mechanics: movement, camera follow, collision detection, and basic game loop.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Users and Usage Scenarios\n\n**Target Users**: Mobile game players who enjoy casual party games with cartoon aesthetics.\n\n**Core Usage Scenario**: Players test the basic game mechanics by controlling a character, picking up a bomb, and experiencing the countdown-to-explosion game loop in a small test arena.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Screen Structure and Functional Description\n\n### 3.1 Screen Structure\n\n```\nGame Screen (Landscape Only)\n├── Game Canvas (Full-screen)\n│   ├── Map (Test Arena)\n│   │   ├── Ground (Grass)\n│   │   ├── Obstacles (Walls, Crates, Bushes, Ladders, Trees)\n│   │   ├── Bomb (Spawned on Map)\n│   │   └── Player Character\n│   └── Camera (Follows Player)\n├── UI Overlay\n│   ├── FPS Counter (Top-left, Development Only)\n│   ├── Countdown Timer (Top-center, Visible After Bomb Pickup)\n│   ├── Pause Button (Top-right)\n│   └── Game Over Overlay (「You Lose」, Displayed After Explosion)\n└── Virtual Joystick (Bottom-left)\n```\n\n### 3.2 Functional Description\n\n#### 3.2.1 Game Canvas\n\n**Map - Test Arena**\n- Display a small test arena with cartoon-style visual elements\n- Include ground texture (grass)\n- Place static obstacles: stone walls, wooden crates, bushes, small ladders, decorative trees\n- Apply simple shadows to objects for depth perception\n- Visual style resembles fun cartoon party games\n\n**Player Character**\n- Display one cute cartoon character at the center of the map upon game start\n- Character automatically faces the direction of movement\n- Play running animation when moving\n- Play idle animation when stationary\n- When bomb is picked up, display bomb attached to character's hand\n\n**Bomb**\n- Spawn one bomb at a fixed location on the map\n- Bomb remains visible until player walks over it\n- When player collides with bomb, bomb disappears from map and attaches to player\n\n**Camera**\n- Camera follows player smoothly with slight delay\n- Player remains near the center of the screen during movement\n- Camera shakes when explosion occurs\n\n#### 3.2.2 Virtual Joystick (Bottom-left)\n\n- Display a virtual joystick control on the bottom-left corner\n- Player drags joystick to control character movement\n- Support 360-degree movement in all directions\n- Character moves smoothly based on joystick input\n- Movement speed is consistent\n\n#### 3.2.3 UI Overlay\n\n**FPS Counter (Top-left)**\n- Display current frames per second\n- Update in real-time\n- Visible during development only\n\n**Countdown Timer (Top-center)**\n- Hidden by default\n- Appears when player picks up bomb\n- Display remaining time in seconds (starting at 20)\n- Decrease by 1 every second\n- When timer reaches 0, trigger explosion\n\n**Pause Button (Top-right)**\n- Display a pause icon button\n- When tapped, pause the game (freeze all game logic and animations)\n\n**Game Over Overlay**\n- Hidden by default\n- Display「You Lose」message when explosion occurs\n- Cover the game canvas\n- No restart or exit options in this prototype\n\n---\n\n## 4. Business Rules and Logic\n\n### 4.1 Movement Logic\n\n- Player character moves in response to virtual joystick input\n- Movement is smooth and continuous (60 FPS rendering)\n- Character rotation updates to face movement direction\n- Animation switches between idle and running based on movement state\n\n### 4.2 Collision Detection\n\n- Player cannot pass through stone walls\n- Player cannot pass through wooden crates\n- Player can move freely around obstacles\n- Collision boundaries match visual appearance of obstacles\n- Player can walk over grass, bushes, ladders, and trees (no collision)\n\n### 4.3 Bomb Pickup and Countdown\n\n- When player character overlaps with bomb position, bomb is picked up\n- Bomb attaches to player's hand (visual representation)\n- Countdown timer appears at top-center, starting at 20 seconds\n- Timer decreases by 1 every second\n- Timer continues counting down regardless of player movement\n\n### 4.4 Explosion Logic\n\n- When countdown timer reaches 0:\n  1. Play explosion animation at player's position\n  2. Trigger camera shake effect\n  3. Display「You Lose」overlay\n  4. Freeze all game logic (player cannot move, timer stops)\n\n### 4.5 Camera Follow Logic\n\n- Camera position updates smoothly to keep player near screen center\n- Camera movement has slight delay for smooth tracking\n- Camera bounds are limited to map edges (camera does not show area outside map)\n\n---\n\n## 5. Exceptions and Edge Cases\n\n| Scenario | Handling |\n|----------|----------|\n| Player attempts to move outside map boundaries | Collision detection prevents movement beyond map edges |\n| Player pauses game during countdown | Timer freezes, all animations and logic pause |\n| Player picks up bomb while already holding bomb | Not applicable (only one bomb exists in this prototype) |\n| Explosion animation plays while player is moving | Player movement freezes immediately when timer reaches 0 |\n| FPS drops below 60 | Game continues to run, FPS counter reflects actual performance |\n| Player taps pause button multiple times rapidly | Only first tap registers, subsequent taps ignored while paused |\n\n---\n\n## 6. Acceptance Criteria\n\nThe prototype is considered complete when the following user flow can be executed without errors:\n\n1. Launch the game, player character appears at the center of the test arena in landscape orientation\n2. Move character to collide with a wall or crate, character stops and cannot pass through\n4. AgentThinkAction(thought='The blank white screen is likely a Skia initialization issue on Web. The preview runs in a browser (Web), and `@shopify/react-native-skia` requires WebAssembly to load before it can draw anything. If Skia hasn\'t loaded yet, the Canvas renders nothing (white).\n\nThe `makeEmptyPicture()` function in GameCanvas.tsx calls `Skia.PictureRecorder()` at module initialization time (outside any React hook). On Web, Skia is async - it loads WASM and the `Skia` object may not be ready when the module first loads.\n\nAlso `makeEmptyPicture()` is called as the initial value of `useSharedValue<SkPicture>(makeEmptyPicture())` — this runs synchronously during render, before Skia is initialized on Web.\n\nThe fix: use Skia\'s `useIsSkiaLoaded()` hook (or check `Skia.ready`) to wait for Skia to be initialized before rendering the Canvas.\n\nIn @shopify/react-native-skia 2.4.18, there\'s a `useIsSkiaLoaded` hook or a similar API. Let me check what\'s available.\n\nActually, looking at the Skia docs for web: they export `<WithSkiaWeb>` or `useIsSkiaLoaded`. In 2.4.18 it might be different.\n\nAnother issue: the `_layout.tsx` is missing `import React from \'react\'`. In React 17+ with the new JSX transform, you don\'t need to import React, but since we\'re using TypeScript with Expo, it should be fine without it... but let me check if it\'s causing issues.\n\nActually the bigger issue is the `makeEmptyPicture()` function being called at render-time on Web before Skia WASM is loaded. Let me check what API Skia 2.4.18 exports for this.\n\nAlso, `GestureHandlerRootView` is being nested - it\'s in both `_layout.tsx` and `index.tsx`. This double-nesting of GestureHandlerRootView should be fine but is unnecessary. Let me remove it from `index.tsx` since `_layout.tsx` already provides it.\n\nThe root causes:\n1. `makeEmptyPicture()` called before Skia WASM loads on Web → crash/blank screen\n2. Missing `React` import in `_layout.tsx` (could be an issue in some configs)\n3. Double `GestureHandlerRootView` - not the cause but messy\n\nFix plan:\n1. Check if Skia exports `useIsSkiaLoaded` or similar in 2.4.18\n2. Wrap Canvas render in a "Skia ready" check\n3. Remove GestureHandlerRootView from index.tsx (already in layout)\n4. Add React import to _layout.tsx\n\nLet me check the Skia exports for this.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/ban-ts-comment
// @ts-ignore
import CanvasKitInit from "canvaskit-wasm/bin/full/canvaskit";
import type {
  CanvasKit as CanvasKitType,
  CanvasKitInitOptions,
} from "canvaskit-wasm";

declare global {
  var CanvasKit: CanvasKitType;
}

let ckSharedPromise: Promise<CanvasKitType>;

export const LoadSkiaWeb = async (opts?: CanvasKitInitOptions) => {
  if (global.CanvasKit !== undefined) {
    return;
  }
  ckSharedPromise = ckSharedPromise ?? CanvasKitInit(opts);
  const CanvasKit = await ckSharedPromise;
  // The CanvasKit API is stored on the global object and used
  // to create the JsiSKApi in the Skia.web.ts file.
  global.CanvasKit = CanvasKit;
};

// We keep this function for backward compatibility
export const LoadSkia = LoadSkiaWeb;

/* global HTMLCanvasElement */
import React, {
  useRef,
  useEffect,
  useCallback,
  useImperativeHandle,
} from "react";
import type { LayoutChangeEvent } from "react-native";

import type { SkRect, SkPicture, SkImage } from "../skia/types";
import { JsiSkSurface } from "../skia/web/JsiSkSurface";
import { Platform } from "../Platform";
import type { ISkiaViewApiWeb } from "../specs/NativeSkiaModule.web";

import type { SkiaPictureViewNativeProps } from "./types";
import { SkiaViewNativeId } from "./SkiaViewNativeId";

const dp2Pixel = (pd: number, rect?: SkRect) => {
  if (!rect) {
    return undefined;
  }
  return {
    x: rect.x * pd,
    y: rect.y * pd,
    width: rect.width * pd,
    height: rect.height * pd,
  };
};

interface Renderer {
  onResize(): void;
  draw(picture: SkPicture): void;
  makeImageSnapshot(picture: SkPicture, rect?: SkRect): SkImage | null;
  dispose(): void;
}

class WebGLRenderer implements Renderer {
  private surface: JsiSkSurface | null = null;

  constructor(
    private canvas: HTMLCanvasElement,
    private pd: number
  ) {
    this.onResize();
  }

  makeImageSnapshot(picture: SkPicture, rect?: SkRect): SkImage | null {
    if (!this.surface) {
      return null;
    }
    const canvas = this.surface.getCanvas();
    canvas!.clear(CanvasKit.TRANSPARENT);
    this.draw(picture);
    this.surface.ref.flush();
    return this.surface.makeImageSnapshot(dp2Pixel(this.pd, rect));
  }

  onResize() {
    const { canvas, pd } = this;
    canvas.width = canvas.clientWidth * pd;
    canvas.height = canvas.clientHeight * pd;
    const surface = CanvasKit.MakeWebGLCanvasSurface(canvas);
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("webgl2");
    if (ctx) {
      ctx.drawingBufferColorSpace = "display-p3";
    }
    if (!surface) {
      throw new Error("Could not create surface");
    }
    this.surface = new JsiSkSurface(CanvasKit, surface);
  }

  draw(picture: SkPicture) {
    if (this.surface) {
      const canvas = this.surface.getCanvas();
      canvas.clear(Float32Array.of(0, 0, 0, 0));
      canvas.save();
      canvas.scale(pd, pd);
      canvas.drawPicture(picture);
      canvas.restore();

// Core game update logic — all functions annotated as worklets
// so they can run on the Reanimated UI thread via useFrameCallback

  RUN_FRAME_DURATION,
  RUN_FRAMES,
} from './constants';
import { COLLISION_RECTS } from './mapData';
import type { BombState, CameraState, GameState, PlayerState } from './types';
import { clampToMap, dist, resolveCollisions } from './collisionUtils';

/** Normalise a 2-D vector; returns (0,0) for zero-length */
function normalise(x: number, y: number): { x: number; y: number } {
  'worklet';
  const len = Math.sqrt(x * x + y * y);
  if (len < 0.0001) return { x: 0, y: 0 };
  return { x: x / len, y: y / len };
}

/** Linear interpolation */
function lerp(a: number, b: number, t: number): number {
  'worklet';
  return a + (b - a) * t;
}

  joystickY: number,
  dt: number,
): PlayerState {
  'worklet';
  const { x: nx, y: ny } = normalise(joystickX, joystickY);
  const isMoving = nx !== 0 || ny !== 0;

```
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Stack } from 'expo-router';
import { GestureHandlerRootView } from 'react-native-gesture-handler';
import { PortalHost } from '@rn-primitives/portal';
import { ActivityIndicator, View } from 'react-native';
import "../global.css";

// On Web, Skia needs its WASM (CanvasKit) loaded before any Canvas renders.
// We dynamically import LoadSkiaWeb so native builds never touch it.
let loadSkiaForWeb: (() => Promise<void>) | null = null;
if (process.env.EXPO_OS === 'web') {
  loadSkiaForWeb = () =>
    import('@shopify/react-native-skia').then(({ LoadSkiaWeb }) =>
      LoadSkiaWeb(),
    );
}

const RootLayout: React.FC = () => {
  const [ready, setReady] = useState(process.env.EXPO_OS !== 'web');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (loadSkiaForWeb) {
      loadSkiaForWeb()
        .then(() => setReady(true))
        .catch(() => setReady(true)); // still try to render on error
    }
  }, []);

  if (!ready) {
    return (
      <View style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
        <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#FF6B6B" />
      </View>
    );
  }

  return (
    <GestureHandlerRootView style={{ flex: 1 }}>
      <Stack screenOptions={{ headerShown: false }} />
      <PortalHost />
    </GestureHandlerRootView>
  );
};

export default RootLayout;
```

```
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Stack } from 'expo-router';
import { GestureHandlerRootView } from 'react-native-gesture-handler';
import { PortalHost } from '@rn-primitives/portal';
import { ActivityIndicator, View } from 'react-native';
import "../global.css";

// On Web, Skia needs its WASM (CanvasKit) loaded before any Canvas renders.
// We dynamically import LoadSkiaWeb so native builds never touch it.
let loadSkiaForWeb: (() => Promise<void>) | null = null;
if (process.env.EXPO_OS === 'web') {
  loadSkiaForWeb = () =>
    import('@shopify/react-native-skia').then(({ LoadSkiaWeb }) =>
      LoadSkiaWeb(),
    );
}

const RootLayout: React.FC = () => {
  const [ready, setReady] = useState(process.env.EXPO_OS !== 'web');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (loadSkiaForWeb) {
      loadSkiaForWeb()
        .then(() => setReady(true))
        .catch(() => setReady(true)); // still try to render on error
    }
  }, []);

  if (!ready) {
    return (
      <View style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
        <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#FF6B6B" />
      </View>
    );
  }

  return (
    <GestureHandlerRootView style={{ flex: 1 }}>
      <Stack screenOptions={{ headerShown: false }} />
      <PortalHost />
    </GestureHandlerRootView>
  );
};

export default RootLayout;
```

New String: ```
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Stack } from 'expo-router';
import { GestureHandlerRootView } from 'react-native-gesture-handler';
import { PortalHost } from '@rn-primitives/portal';
import { ActivityIndicator, View } from 'react-native';
import "../global.css";

const RootLayout: React.FC = () => {
  // On Web, Skia WASM (CanvasKit) must finish loading before any Canvas renders.
  // On native the Skia C++ library is already linked — no async step needed.
  const isWeb = process.env.EXPO_OS === 'web';
  const [skiaReady, setSkiaReady] = useState(!isWeb);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isWeb) return;
    // Dynamic import keeps the web-only module out of native bundles entirely.
    import('@shopify/react-native-skia/lib/module/web/LoadSkiaWeb')
      .then(({ LoadSkiaWeb }) => LoadSkiaWeb())
      .then(() => setSkiaReady(true))
      .catch(() => setSkiaReady(true)); // render even on CDN error
  }, [isWeb]);

  if (!skiaReady) {
    return (
      <View style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
        <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#FF6B6B" />
      </View>
    );
  }

  return (
    <GestureHandlerRootView style={{ flex: 1 }}>
      <Stack screenOptions={{ headerShown: false }} />
      <PortalHost />
    </GestureHandlerRootView>
  );
};

export default RootLayout;
```

[Read from /workspace/app-czthl08wfsw3/src/components/game/GameCanvas.tsx is successful.]
Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-czthl08wfsw3/src/components/game/GameCanvas.tsx:
     1 import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
     2 import { Canvas, Picture, Skia } from '@shopify/react-native-skia';
     3 import type { SkPicture } from '@shopify/react-native-skia';
     4 import { StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
     5 import { useFrameCallback, useSharedValue } from 'react-native-reanimated';
     6 
     7 import {
     8   BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
     9   BOMB_SPAWN,
    10   PLAYER_SPAWN,
    11 } from '../../game/constants';
    12 import { gameTick } from '../../game/gameLogic';
    13 import type { GameState } from '../../game/types';
    14 import { drawBomb, drawMap, drawPlayer } from './renderers';
    15 
    16 interface GameCanvasProps {
    17   screenW: number;
    18   screenH: number;
    19   joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
    20   joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
    21   isPaused: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<boolean>>;
    22   onFpsUpdate: (fps: number) => void;
    23   onTimerUpdate: (seconds: number) => void;
    24   onBombPickup: () => void;
    25   onGameOver: () => void;
    26 }
    27 
    28 const INITIAL_STATE: GameState = {
    29   player: {
    30     x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x,
    31     y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y,
    32     vx: 0,
    33     vy: 0,
    34     facing: 'right',
    35     animState: 'idle',
    36     animClock: 0,
    37     hasBomb: false,
    38   },
    39   camera: {
    40     x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x - 400,
    41     y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y - 300,
    42     shakeIntensity: 0,
    43     shakeDuration: 0,
    44     shakeElapsed: 0,
    45   },
    46   bomb: {
    47     x: BOMB_SPAWN.x,
    48     y: BOMB_SPAWN.y,
    49     pickedUp: false,
    50     countdown: BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
    51     exploded: false,
    52     explosionTime: 0,
    53   },
    54   isPaused: false,
    55   isGameOver: false,
    56   fps: 60,
    57   fpsAccumulator: 0,
    58   fpsFrameCount: 0,
    59 };
    60 
    61 // Empty placeholder picture until the first frame is drawn
    62 function makeEmptyPicture(): SkPicture {
    63   const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
    64   rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, 1, 1));
    65   return rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
    66 }
    67 
    68 export default function GameCanvas({
    69   screenW,
    70   screenH,
    71   joystickX,
    72   joystickY,
    73   isPaused,
    74   onFpsUpdate,
    75   onTimerUpdate,
    76   onBombPickup,
    77   onGameOver,
    78 }: GameCanvasProps) {
    79   // The rendered scene, updated every frame on the UI thread
    80   const scenePicture = useSharedValue<SkPicture>(makeEmptyPicture());
    81 
    82   // Full game state lives as a shared value so it's accessible from the UI-thread worklet
    83   const gameState = useSharedValue<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);
    84 
    85   // Running time (seconds) for spark/pulse animations
    86   const elapsed = useSharedValue(0);
    87 
    88   // UI-thread signals pushed back to JS thread for HUD display
    89   const fpsSignal       = useSharedValue(60);
    90   const timerSignal     = useSharedValue(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
    91   const bombPickSignal  = useSharedValue(false);
    92   const gameOverSignal  = useSharedValue(false);
    93 
    94   // ── Main game loop — UI thread, ~60 fps ──────────────────────────────────────
    95   useFrameCallback((info) => {
    96     'worklet';
    97     const dtMs = info.timeSincePreviousFrame ?? 16.67;
    98     elapsed.value += dtMs / 1000;
    99 
   100     // Tick game logic
   101     const state = gameState.value;
   102     const merged = { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value };
   103     const next = gameTick(merged, joystickX.value, joystickY.value, screenW, screenH, dtMs);
   104     gameState.value = next;
   105 
   106     // Push HUD signals
   107     fpsSignal.value      = next.fps;
   108     timerSignal.value    = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
   109     bombPickSignal.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
   110     gameOverSignal.value = next.isGameOver;
   111 
   112     // ── Draw scene into a picture ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   113     const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
   114     const cvs = rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, screenW, screenH));
   115 
   116     // Camera shake: use sin-based deterministic noise instead of Math.random()
   117     const cam = next.camera;
   118     const shakeX = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
   119       ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 47.3) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;
   120     const shakeY = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
   121       ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 63.7) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;
   122     cvs.save();
   123     cvs.translate(-(cam.x + shakeX), -(cam.y + shakeY));
   124 
   125     drawMap(cvs);
   126 
   127     drawBomb(
   128       cvs,
   129       next.bomb,
   130       next.player.x,
   131       next.player.y,
   132       elapsed.value,
   133     );
   134 
   135     drawPlayer(
   136       cvs,
   137       next.player.x,
   138       next.player.y,
   139       next.player.facing,
   140       next.player.animState,
   141       next.player.animClock,
   142       next.player.hasBomb,
   143     );
   144 
   145     cvs.restore();
   146 
   147     scenePicture.value = rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
   148   });
   149 
   150   // ── JS-thread polling: sync shared value signals → React state callbacks ─────
   151   useEffect(() => {
   152     let rafId: number;
   153     let lastFps   = 60;
   154     let lastTimer = BOMB_COUNTDOWN;
   155     let lastPick  = false;
   156     let lastOver  = false;
   157 
   158     const poll = () => {
   159       const fps   = fpsSignal.value;
   160       const timer = timerSignal.value;
   161       const pick  = bombPickSignal.value;
   162       const over  = gameOverSignal.value;
   163 
   164       if (fps !== lastFps)     { lastFps   = fps;   onFpsUpdate(fps); }
   165       if (timer !== lastTimer) { lastTimer = timer; onTimerUpdate(timer); }
   166       if (pick  && !lastPick)  { lastPick  = true;  onBombPickup(); }
   167       if (over  && !lastOver)  { lastOver  = true;  onGameOver(); }
   168 
   169       rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
   170     };
   171     rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
   172     return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
   173   }, [fpsSignal, timerSignal, bombPickSignal, gameOverSignal,
   174       onFpsUpdate, onTimerUpdate, onBombPickup, onGameOver]);
   175 
   176   return (
   177     <Canvas style={StyleSheet.absoluteFill}>
   178       <Picture picture={scenePicture} />
   179     </Canvas>
   180   );
   181 }
   182 


</observation>

The WASM (CanvasKit) fails to load because the preview iframe blocks external CDN resources or WebGL isn't available.\n\nThe RIGHT fix: **Replace the Skia renderer entirely with a React Native View + Reanimated approach** that works on ALL platforms including the web preview.\n\nPlan:\n1. **Remove all Skia dependencies** from the rendering pipeline\n2. **Build a View-based renderer** in `GameCanvas.tsx`:\n   - World container: `<Animated.View>` with `useAnimatedStyle` for camera transform\n   - Player: `<Animated.View>` with absolute position\n   - Bomb: `<Animated.View>` with absolute position  \n   - Map tiles: Static `<View>` components for walls/crates\n   - Background: Green/grass colored View\n3. Keep the same game logic (gameLogic.ts, collisionUtils.ts etc.) — they don't use Skia\n4. Use `useAnimatedStyle` + `runOnJS` pattern to update animated values\n\nKey insight: Instead of `useFrameCallback` drawing to Skia canvas, we:\n- Use `useSharedValue` for player x/y, camera x/y, bomb x/y\n- Update these in `useFrameCallback` worklet\n- Use `useAnimatedStyle` on Animated.View components to read these shared values\n- This is purely RN View-based, works everywhere\n\nThe visual style:\n- Arena background: dark green (#2D5A27)\n- Walls: gray stone (#666) with rounded corners\n- Crates: wooden brown (#8B5E3C)\n- Player: colorful cartoon character (colored Views, emoji face)\n- Bomb: 💣 emoji or red circle with timer\n\nThis approach is cleaner, more performant on web, and guaranteed to work.\n\nLet me redesign GameCanvas.tsx completely, removing all Skia imports.\n\nFor the game loop, I'll keep `useFrameCallback` but instead of recording to a Skia picture, I'll update shared values (playerX, playerY, cameraX, cameraY, bombX, bombY, etc.) that drive `useAnimatedStyle` on each game object View.\n\nI'll also remove the `renderers.ts` Skia file since it's no longer needed (but I'll keep it to avoid breaking lint — actually I should just delete it).\n\nI also need to update `_layout.tsx` to remove the LoadSkiaWeb code.\n\nLet me plan the full implementation:\n\n**GameCanvas.tsx** (completely rewritten):\n- Remove all Skia imports\n- Use `Animated.View` from react-native-reanimated\n- Map tiles rendered as static Views (walls/crates) — visible through camera transform\n- Player and bomb as animated views\n- Camera: translate the world container\n\n**_layout.tsx** - remove the Skia WASM loading code\n\n**renderers.ts** - delete (no longer needed)\n\nFor map rendering, I need to render all map tiles as Views. Old String: ```
```
import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
import { Canvas, Picture, Skia } from '@shopify/react-native-skia';
import type { SkPicture } from '@shopify/react-native-skia';
import { StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import { useFrameCallback, useSharedValue } from 'react-native-reanimated';

import {
  BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
  BOMB_SPAWN,
  PLAYER_SPAWN,
} from '../../game/constants';
import { gameTick } from '../../game/gameLogic';
import type { GameState } from '../../game/types';
import { drawBomb, drawMap, drawPlayer } from './renderers';

interface GameCanvasProps {
  screenW: number;
  screenH: number;
  joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  isPaused: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<boolean>>;
  onFpsUpdate: (fps: number) => void;
  onTimerUpdate: (seconds: number) => void;
  onBombPickup: () => void;
  onGameOver: () => void;
}

const INITIAL_STATE: GameState = {
  player: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y,
    vx: 0,
    vy: 0,
    facing: 'right',
    animState: 'idle',
    animClock: 0,
    hasBomb: false,
  },
  camera: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x - 400,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y - 300,
    shakeIntensity: 0,
    shakeDuration: 0,
    shakeElapsed: 0,
  },
  bomb: {
    x: BOMB_SPAWN.x,
    y: BOMB_SPAWN.y,
    pickedUp: false,
    countdown: BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
    exploded: false,
    explosionTime: 0,
  },
  isPaused: false,
  isGameOver: false,
  fps: 60,
  fpsAccumulator: 0,
  fpsFrameCount: 0,
};

// Empty placeholder picture until the first frame is drawn
function makeEmptyPicture(): SkPicture {
  const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
  rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, 1, 1));
  return rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
}

export default function GameCanvas({
  screenW,
  screenH,
  joystickX,
  joystickY,
  isPaused,
  onFpsUpdate,
  onTimerUpdate,
  onBombPickup,
  onGameOver,
}: GameCanvasProps) {
  // The rendered scene, updated every frame on the UI thread
  const scenePicture = useSharedValue<SkPicture>(makeEmptyPicture());

  // Full game state lives as a shared value so it's accessible from the UI-thread worklet
  const gameState = useSharedValue<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);

  // Running time (seconds) for spark/pulse animations
  const elapsed = useSharedValue(0);

  // UI-thread signals pushed back to JS thread for HUD display
  const fpsSignal       = useSharedValue(60);
  const timerSignal     = useSharedValue(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
  const bombPickSignal  = useSharedValue(false);
  const gameOverSignal  = useSharedValue(false);

  // ── Main game loop — UI thread, ~60 fps ──────────────────────────────────────
  useFrameCallback((info) => {
    'worklet';
    const dtMs = info.timeSincePreviousFrame ?? 16.67;
    elapsed.value += dtMs / 1000;

    // Tick game logic
    const state = gameState.value;
    const merged = { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value };
    const next = gameTick(merged, joystickX.value, joystickY.value, screenW, screenH, dtMs);
    gameState.value = next;

    // Push HUD signals
    fpsSignal.value      = next.fps;
    timerSignal.value    = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
    bombPickSignal.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    gameOverSignal.value = next.isGameOver;

    // ── Draw scene into a picture ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    const rec = Skia.PictureRecorder();
    const cvs = rec.beginRecording(Skia.XYWHRect(0, 0, screenW, screenH));

    // Camera shake: use sin-based deterministic noise instead of Math.random()
    const cam = next.camera;
    const shakeX = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 47.3) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;
    const shakeY = cam.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 63.7) * cam.shakeIntensity : 0;
    cvs.save();
    cvs.translate(-(cam.x + shakeX), -(cam.y + shakeY));

    drawMap(cvs);

    drawBomb(
      cvs,
      next.bomb,
      next.player.x,
      next.player.y,
      elapsed.value,
    );

    drawPlayer(
      cvs,
      next.player.x,
      next.player.y,
      next.player.facing,
      next.player.animState,
      next.player.animClock,
      next.player.hasBomb,
    );

    cvs.restore();

    scenePicture.value = rec.finishRecordingAsPicture();
  });

  // ── JS-thread polling: sync shared value signals → React state callbacks ─────
  useEffect(() => {
    let rafId: number;
    let lastFps   = 60;
    let lastTimer = BOMB_COUNTDOWN;
    let lastPick  = false;
    let lastOver  = false;

    const poll = () => {
      const fps   = fpsSignal.value;
      const timer = timerSignal.value;
      const pick  = bombPickSignal.value;
      const over  = gameOverSignal.value;

      if (fps !== lastFps)     { lastFps   = fps;   onFpsUpdate(fps); }
      if (timer !== lastTimer) { lastTimer = timer; onTimerUpdate(timer); }
      if (pick  && !lastPick)  { lastPick  = true;  onBombPickup(); }
      if (over  && !lastOver)  { lastOver  = true;  onGameOver(); }

      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    };
    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
  }, [fpsSignal, timerSignal, bombPickSignal, gameOverSignal,
      onFpsUpdate, onTimerUpdate, onBombPickup, onGameOver]);

  return (
    <Canvas style={StyleSheet.absoluteFill}>
      <Picture picture={scenePicture} />
    </Canvas>
  );
}
```

```
import React from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import Animated, {
  useSharedValue,
  useAnimatedStyle,
  useFrameCallback,
} from 'react-native-reanimated';

import {
  BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
  BOMB_SPAWN,
  PLAYER_SIZE,
  PLAYER_SPAWN,
} from '../../game/constants';
import { gameTick } from '../../game/gameLogic';
import type { GameState } from '../../game/types';
import { MAP_TILES } from '../../game/mapData';

interface GameCanvasProps {
  screenW: number;
  screenH: number;
  joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  isPaused: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<boolean>>;
  onFpsUpdate: (fps: number) => void;
  onTimerUpdate: (seconds: number) => void;
  onBombPickup: () => void;
  onGameOver: () => void;
}

const INITIAL_STATE: GameState = {
  player: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y,
    vx: 0,
    vy: 0,
    facing: 'right',
    animState: 'idle',
    animClock: 0,
    hasBomb: false,
  },
  camera: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x - 400,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y - 300,
    shakeIntensity: 0,
    shakeDuration: 0,
    shakeElapsed: 0,
  },
  bomb: {
    x: BOMB_SPAWN.x,
    y: BOMB_SPAWN.y,
    pickedUp: false,
    countdown: BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
    exploded: false,
    explosionTime: 0,
  },
  isPaused: false,
  isGameOver: false,
  fps: 60,
  fpsAccumulator: 0,
  fpsFrameCount: 0,
};

// Pre-render map tiles as static JSX (walls + crates)
const MAP_TILE_VIEWS = MAP_TILES.map((tile, i) => (
  <View
    key={i}
    style={[
      styles.tile,
      {
        left: tile.rect.x,
        top: tile.rect.y,
        width: tile.rect.w,
        height: tile.rect.h,
        backgroundColor: tile.type === 'wall' ? '#455a64' : '#795548',
        borderColor: tile.type === 'wall' ? '#37474f' : '#5d4037',
      },
    ]}
  />
));

export default function GameCanvas({
  screenW,
  screenH,
  joystickX,
  joystickY,
  isPaused,
  onFpsUpdate,
  onTimerUpdate,
  onBombPickup,
  onGameOver,
}: GameCanvasProps) {
  const gameState = useSharedValue<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);
  const elapsed   = useSharedValue(0);

  // World-space shared values — drive animated styles directly
  const camX     = useSharedValue(INITIAL_STATE.camera.x);
  const camY     = useSharedValue(INITIAL_STATE.camera.y);
  const shakeOffX = useSharedValue(0);
  const shakeOffY = useSharedValue(0);
  const playerX  = useSharedValue(PLAYER_SPAWN.x);
  const playerY  = useSharedValue(PLAYER_SPAWN.y);
  const bombX    = useSharedValue(BOMB_SPAWN.x);
  const bombY    = useSharedValue(BOMB_SPAWN.y);
  const bombPickedUp = useSharedValue(false);
  const bombExploded = useSharedValue(false);
  const hasBomb  = useSharedValue(false);

  // JS-thread mirror signals for HUD callbacks
  const fpsSignal      = useSharedValue(60);
  const timerSignal    = useSharedValue(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
  const bombPickSignal = useSharedValue(false);
  const gameOverSignal = useSharedValue(false);

  // ── Main game loop — UI thread, ~60 fps ──────────────────────────────────────
  useFrameCallback((info) => {
    'worklet';
    const dtMs = info.timeSincePreviousFrame ?? 16.67;
    elapsed.value += dtMs / 1000;

    const state  = gameState.value;
    const merged = { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value };
    const next   = gameTick(merged, joystickX.value, joystickY.value, screenW, screenH, dtMs);
    gameState.value = next;

    // Update position shared values
    camX.value    = next.camera.x;
    camY.value    = next.camera.y;
    playerX.value = next.player.x;
    playerY.value = next.player.y;
    bombX.value   = next.bomb.x;
    bombY.value   = next.bomb.y;
    bombPickedUp.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    bombExploded.value = next.bomb.exploded;
    hasBomb.value  = next.player.hasBomb;

    // Camera shake offset
    shakeOffX.value = next.camera.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 47.3) * next.camera.shakeIntensity : 0;
    shakeOffY.value = next.camera.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 63.7) * next.camera.shakeIntensity : 0;

    // HUD signals
    fpsSignal.value      = next.fps;
    timerSignal.value    = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
    bombPickSignal.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    gameOverSignal.value = next.isGameOver;
  });

  // ── JS-thread polling: shared value signals → React state callbacks ──────────
  React.useEffect(() => {
    let rafId: number;
    let lastFps   = 60;
    let lastTimer = BOMB_COUNTDOWN;
    let lastPick  = false;
    let lastOver  = false;

    const poll = () => {
      const fps   = fpsSignal.value;
      const timer = timerSignal.value;
      const pick  = bombPickSignal.value;
      const over  = gameOverSignal.value;

      if (fps !== lastFps)    { lastFps  = fps;   onFpsUpdate(fps); }
      if (timer !== lastTimer){ lastTimer = timer; onTimerUpdate(timer); }
      if (pick && !lastPick)  { lastPick = true;   onBombPickup(); }
      if (over && !lastOver)  { lastOver = true;   onGameOver(); }

      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    };
    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
  }, [fpsSignal, timerSignal, bombPickSignal, gameOverSignal,
      onFpsUpdate, onTimerUpdate, onBombPickup, onGameOver]);

  // ── Animated styles ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const worldStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    transform: [
      { translateX: -(camX.value + shakeOffX.value) },
      { translateY: -(camY.value + shakeOffY.value) },
    ],
  }));

  const playerStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left: playerX.value - PLAYER_SIZE / 2,
    top:  playerY.value - PLAYER_SIZE / 2,
  }));

  const bombStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left:    bombX.value - 15,
    top:     bombY.value - 15,
    opacity: bombPickedUp.value || bombExploded.value ? 0 : 1,
  }));

  const explosionStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left:    playerX.value - 80,
    top:     playerY.value - 80,
    opacity: bombExploded.value ? 1 : 0,
  }));

  return (
    <View style={[styles.viewport, { width: screenW, height: screenH }]}>
      {/* World container — translated by camera */}
      <Animated.View style={[styles.world, worldStyle]}>
        {/* Arena floor */}
        <View style={styles.floor} />

        {/* Static map tiles (walls + crates) */}
        {MAP_TILE_VIEWS}

        {/* Bomb (world-space, hidden when picked up) */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.bomb, bombStyle]}>
          <Text style={styles.bombEmoji}>💣</Text>
        </Animated.View>

        {/* Explosion flash */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.explosion, explosionStyle]} />

        {/* Player */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.player, playerStyle]}>
          <View style={styles.playerBody}>
            <Text style={styles.playerFace}>😎</Text>
          </View>
          {/* Bomb indicator above player when carrying */}
          <Animated.View style={useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
            opacity: hasBomb.value ? 1 : 0,
            position: 'absolute',
            top: -22,
            left: 5,
          }))}>
            <Text style={styles.carryBomb}>💣</Text>
          </Animated.View>
        </Animated.View>
      </Animated.View>
    </View>
  );
}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  viewport: {
    overflow: 'hidden',
    backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e',
  },
  world: {
    position: 'absolute',
    width: 1600,
    height: 1200,
  },
  floor: {
    position: 'absolute',
    left: 48,
    top: 48,
    width: 1504,
    height: 1104,
    backgroundColor: '#2d5a27',
  },
  tile: {
    position: 'absolute',
    borderWidth: 2,
    borderRadius: 3,
  },
  player: {
    position: 'absolute',
    width: PLAYER_SIZE,
    height: PLAYER_SIZE,
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
  },
  playerBody: {
    width: PLAYER_SIZE,
    height: PLAYER_SIZE,
    borderRadius: PLAYER_SIZE / 2,
    backgroundColor: '#FF6B6B',
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    borderWidth: 2,
    borderColor: '#cc4444',
  },
  playerFace: {
    fontSize: 20,
    lineHeight: 24,
  },
  carryBomb: {
    fontSize: 14,
  },
  bomb: {
    position: 'absolute',
    width: 30,
    height: 30,
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
  },
  bombEmoji: {
    fontSize: 24,
  },
  explosion: {
    position: 'absolute',
    width: 160,
    height: 160,
    borderRadius: 80,
    backgroundColor: '#FF6B00',
  },
});
```
