```
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Stack } from 'expo-router';
import { GestureHandlerRootView } from 'react-native-gesture-handler';
import { PortalHost } from '@rn-primitives/portal';
import { ActivityIndicator, View } from 'react-native';
import "../global.css";

const RootLayout: React.FC = () => {
  // On Web, Skia WASM (CanvasKit) must finish loading before any Canvas renders.
  // On native the Skia C++ library is already linked — no async step needed.
  const isWeb = process.env.EXPO_OS === 'web';
  const [skiaReady, setSkiaReady] = useState(!isWeb);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isWeb) return;
    // Dynamic import keeps the web-only module out of native bundles entirely.
    import('@shopify/react-native-skia/lib/module/web/LoadSkiaWeb')
      .then(({ LoadSkiaWeb }) => LoadSkiaWeb())
      .then(() => setSkiaReady(true))
      .catch(() => setSkiaReady(true)); // render even on CDN error
  }, [isWeb]);

  if (!skiaReady) {
    return (
      <View style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
        <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#FF6B6B" />
      </View>
    );
  }
```

```
  return (
    <GestureHandlerRootView style={{ flex: 1 }}>
      <Stack screenOptions={{ headerShown: false }} />
      <PortalHost />
    </GestureHandlerRootView>
  );
};

export default RootLayout;
```

     1 'worklet';
     2 // Core game update logic — all functions annotated as worklets
     3 // so they can run on the Reanimated UI thread via useFrameCallback
     4 
     5 import {
     6   BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
     7   BOMB_PICKUP_RADIUS,
     8   CAMERA_LERP,
     9   CAMERA_SHAKE_DURATION,
    10   CAMERA_SHAKE_MAGNITUDE,
    11   EXPLOSION_DURATION,
    12   FPS_UPDATE_INTERVAL,
    13   IDLE_FRAME_DURATION,
    14   IDLE_FRAMES,
    15   MAP_HEIGHT,
    16   MAP_WIDTH,
    17   PLAYER_SPEED,
    18   RUN_FRAME_DURATION,
    19   RUN_FRAMES,
    20 } from './constants';
    21 import { COLLISION_RECTS } from './mapData';
    22 import type { BombState, CameraState, GameState, PlayerState } from './types';
    23 import { clampToMap, dist, resolveCollisions } from './collisionUtils';
    24 
    25 /** Normalise a 2-D vector; returns (0,0) for zero-length */
    26 function normalise(x: number, y: number): { x: number; y: number } {
    27   'worklet';
    28   const len = Math.sqrt(x * x + y * y);
    29   if (len < 0.0001) return { x: 0, y: 0 };
    30   return { x: x / len, y: y / len };
    31 }
    32 
    33 /** Linear interpolation */
    34 function lerp(a: number, b: number, t: number): number {
    35   'worklet';
    36   return a + (b - a) * t;
    37 }
    38 
    39 // ─── Player update ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    40 
    41 export function updatePlayer(
    42   player: PlayerState,
    43   joystickX: number,
    44   joystickY: number,
    45   dt: number,
    46 ): PlayerState {
    47   'worklet';
    48   const { x: nx, y: ny } = normalise(joystickX, joystickY);
    49   const isMoving = nx !== 0 || ny !== 0;
    50 
    51   // Velocity
    52   const vx = nx * PLAYER_SPEED;
    53   const vy = ny * PLAYER_SPEED;
    54 
    55   // Proposed new position
    56   let px = player.x + vx * dt;
    57   let py = player.y + vy * dt;
    58 
    59   // Clamp within map first
    60   const clamped = clampToMap(px, py, MAP_WIDTH, MAP_HEIGHT);
    61   px = clamped.px;
    62   py = clamped.py;
    63 
    64   // Resolve solid collisions
    65   const resolved = resolveCollisions(px, py, COLLISION_RECTS);
    66   px = resolved.px;
    67   py = resolved.py;
    68 
    69   // Facing direction (only update when actually moving)
    70   const facing = nx < -0.1 ? 'left' : nx > 0.1 ? 'right' : player.facing;
    71 
    72   // Animation clock
    73   const animState = isMoving ? 'running' : 'idle';
    74   const frameDur = animState === 'running' ? RUN_FRAME_DURATION : IDLE_FRAME_DURATION;
    75   const frameCount = animState === 'running' ? RUN_FRAMES : IDLE_FRAMES;
    76   const animClock = (player.animClock + dt * 1000) % (frameDur * frameCount);
    77 
    78   return {
    79     ...player,
    80     x: px,
    81     y: py,
    82     vx,
    83     vy,
    84     facing,
    85     animState,
    86     animClock,
    87   };
    88 }
    89 
    90 // ─── Camera update ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    91 
    92 export function updateCamera(
    93   camera: CameraState,
    94   targetX: number,
    95   targetY: number,
    96   screenW: number,
    97   screenH: number,
    98   dt: number,
    99 ): CameraState {
   100   'worklet';
   101   // Ideal camera so player is at screen center
   102   const idealX = targetX - screenW / 2;
   103   const idealY = targetY - screenH / 2;
   104 
   105   // Clamp to map edges
   106   const clampedX = Math.max(0, Math.min(MAP_WIDTH  - screenW,  idealX));
   107   const clampedY = Math.max(0, Math.min(MAP_HEIGHT - screenH, idealY));
   108 
   109   const lerpFactor = 1 - Math.pow(1 - CAMERA_LERP, dt * 60);
   110   const cx = lerp(camera.x, clampedX, lerpFactor);
   111   const cy = lerp(camera.y, clampedY, lerpFactor);
   112 
   113   // Shake
   114   let shakeElapsed = camera.shakeElapsed;
   115   let shakeIntensity = camera.shakeIntensity;
   116   if (shakeElapsed < camera.shakeDuration) {
   117     shakeElapsed += dt * 1000;
   118     shakeIntensity = CAMERA_SHAKE_MAGNITUDE * (1 - shakeElapsed / camera.shakeDuration);
   119   } else {
   120     shakeIntensity = 0;
   121   }
   122 
   123   return {
   124     x: cx,
   125     y: cy,
   126     shakeIntensity,
   127     shakeDuration: camera.shakeDuration,
   128     shakeElapsed,
   129   };
   130 }
   131 
   132 /** Trigger camera shake */
   133 export function triggerShake(camera: CameraState): CameraState {
   134   'worklet';
   135   return {
   136     ...camera,
   137     shakeIntensity: CAMERA_SHAKE_MAGNITUDE,
   138     shakeDuration: CAMERA_SHAKE_DURATION,
   139     shakeElapsed: 0,
   140   };
   141 }
   142 
   143 // ─── Bomb update ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   144 
   145 export function updateBomb(
   146   bomb: BombState,
   147   playerX: number,
   148   playerY: number,
   149   dt: number,
   150 ): BombState {
   151   'worklet';
   152   if (bomb.exploded) {
   153     return {
   154       ...bomb,
   155       explosionTime: bomb.explosionTime + dt * 1000,
   156     };
   157   }
   158 
   159   if (!bomb.pickedUp) {
   160     // Check pickup
   161     const d = dist(playerX, playerY, bomb.x, bomb.y);
   162     if (d < BOMB_PICKUP_RADIUS) {
   163       return { ...bomb, pickedUp: true };
   164     }
   165     return bomb;
   166   }
   167 
   168   // Bomb is ticking
   169   const newCountdown = bomb.countdown - dt;
   170   if (newCountdown <= 0) {
   171     return {
   172       ...bomb,
   173       countdown: 0,
   174       exploded: true,
   175       explosionTime: 0,
   176     };
   177   }
   178 
   179   return { ...bomb, countdown: newCountdown };
   180 }
   181 
   182 // ─── FPS counter ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   183 
   184 export function updateFps(
   185   state: GameState,
   186   dt: number,
   187 ): { fps: number; fpsAccumulator: number; fpsFrameCount: number } {
   188   'worklet';
   189   const acc = state.fpsAccumulator + dt * 1000;
   190   const fc = state.fpsFrameCount + 1;
   191 
   192   if (acc >= FPS_UPDATE_INTERVAL) {
   193     return {
   194       fps: Math.round(fc / (acc / 1000)),
   195       fpsAccumulator: 0,
   196       fpsFrameCount: 0,
   197     };
   198   }
   199   return { fps: state.fps, fpsAccumulator: acc, fpsFrameCount: fc };
   200 }
   201 
   202 // ─── Full game tick ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   203 
   204 export function gameTick(
   205   state: GameState,
   206   joystickX: number,
   207   joystickY: number,
   208   screenW: number,
   209   screenH: number,
   210   dtMs: number,
   211 ): GameState {
   212   'worklet';
   213   if (state.isPaused || state.isGameOver) return state;
   214 
   215   const dt = Math.min(dtMs / 1000, 0.05); // cap dt to 50ms
   216 
   217   const fpsResult = updateFps(state, dt);
   218 
   219   let player = updatePlayer(state.player, joystickX, joystickY, dt);
   220 
   221   // Bomb position follows player hand when picked up
   222   let bomb = updateBomb(state.bomb, player.x, player.y, dt);
   223 
   224   // Sync hasBomb flag onto player
   225   if (bomb.pickedUp !== player.hasBomb) {
   226     player = { ...player, hasBomb: bomb.pickedUp };
   227   }
   228 
   229   let camera = updateCamera(state.camera, player.x, player.y, screenW, screenH, dt);
   230 
   231   let isGameOver: boolean = state.isGameOver;
   232 
   233   // Explosion triggers camera shake + game over
   234   if (bomb.exploded && !state.bomb.exploded) {
   235     camera = triggerShake(camera);
   236     isGameOver = true;
   237   }
   238 
   239   // After explosion animation finishes, just keep game over state
   240   const explosionDone = bomb.exploded && bomb.explosionTime >= EXPLOSION_DURATION;
   241 
   242   return {
   243     ...state,
   244     player,
   245     camera,
   246     bomb,
   247     isGameOver: isGameOver || explosionDone,
   248     fps: fpsResult.fps,
   249     fpsAccumulator: fpsResult.fpsAccumulator,
   250     fpsFrameCount: fpsResult.fpsFrameCount,
   251   };
   252 }

The issue is likely one of:\n\n1. **`useFrameCallback` not available in Reanimated 4 on web** - `useFrameCallback` is a Reanimated API. On web, Reanimated might not support it or it might silently fail.\n\n2. **`\'worklet\'` directive on file-level (`gameLogic.ts` line 1)** - This is unusual. Reanimated worklets can have this at function level but a file-level `\'worklet\'` string literal is not standard. When running on web, Reanimated might crash processing this.\n\n3. **Import of `COLLISION_RECTS` from mapData.ts in a worklet** - `gameLogic.ts` imports `COLLISION_RECTS` from `mapData.ts`. This is a module-level import, not a worklet-captured variable. In Reanimated worklets, you can\'t import module-level variables directly in the traditional sense - they need to be captured by closure. However in the `useFrameCallback` in `GameCanvas.tsx`, we call `gameTick` which internally references `COLLISION_RECTS` (imported from `mapData.ts`). This might fail in the worklet context.\n\n4. **`collisionUtils.ts` issues** - Similar module import problems.\n\n5. **The `useAnimatedStyle` with inline function component** - In `GameCanvas.tsx`, there\'s a nested `useAnimatedStyle` inside a JSX element\'s `style` prop:\n```tsx\n<Animated.View style={useAnimatedStyle(() => ({\n  opacity: hasBomb.value ? 1 : 0,\n  position: \'absolute\',\n  top: -22,\n  left: 5,\n}))}>\n```\n**This is ILLEGAL** - you cannot call a hook inside JSX. This would cause a React error: "Rendered more hooks than during the previous render" or "Invalid hook call". This would crash the entire component tree and show a blank screen!\n\nThat\'s the bug! The `hasBomb` `useAnimatedStyle` is called inside JSX (conditional render context of a child component), violating the Rules of Hooks.\n\nAlso, the game is fundamentally complex. Let me think about a simpler approach that DEFINITELY works:\n\n**Simplest approach that will work:**\n- Remove `useFrameCallback` (which requires Reanimated\'s worklet runtime)\n- Remove ALL `\'worklet\'` directives\n- Use a simple `setInterval` or `requestAnimationFrame` loop on the JS thread\n- Use `useState` for player/camera/bomb positions\n- Render with regular React state\n\nThis is the most reliable approach. The game will run at 60fps on JS thread using `requestAnimationFrame`, and since it\'s a simple 2D game with low-complexity logic, this will work fine.\n\nActually, even simpler: just use `useRef` + `requestAnimationFrame` + `setState` with `flushSync` or just a simple `useRef` for the world container with direct style mutations.\n\nWait, even better: use `react-native-reanimated` but WITHOUT worklets. Just use `useSharedValue` + `useAnimatedStyle` on the JS thread:\n- Game loop: regular `requestAnimationFrame` in `useEffect`\n- Position updates: `sharedValue.value = newPos` from JS thread (this triggers the animated style to update on the UI thread)\n\nThis is the correct approach and avoids all worklet complexity.\n\nLet me redesign `GameCanvas.tsx` completely:\n1. Remove `useFrameCallback` → use `useEffect` + `requestAnimationFrame`\n2. Remove all `\'worklet\'` calls to `gameTick` etc.\n3. Keep `useSharedValue` + `useAnimatedStyle` for smooth rendering\n4. Fix the nested `useAnimatedStyle` hook violation\n\nAlso fix `gameLogic.ts`:\n- Remove the file-level `\'worklet\'` string\n- Remove `\'worklet\'` from all functions (since they\'ll be called from JS thread now)\n- Same for `collisionUtils.ts`\n\nActually, I should keep the worklet annotations for when it runs on native (for performance). The issue is that on **web**, Reanimated\'s worklet runtime may not work correctly, and the `useFrameCallback` might silently fail.\n\nActually, the REAL issue might be simpler: Let me check if `useFrameCallback` works on web for Reanimated 4.\n\nIn Reanimated 4, `useFrameCallback` should work on web too. But the `\'worklet\'` directive means the function runs in a separate JS context (the UI thread), and imports inside worklets need to be self-contained.\n\nThe most critical bug I spotted: **nested `useAnimatedStyle` inside JSX** - this is a Rules of Hooks violation that would crash the component.\n\nLet me fix this specifically:\n```tsx\n// WRONG - hook inside JSX\n<Animated.View style={useAnimatedStyle(() => ({...}))}>\n```\n\nFix: extract `hasBombStyle` as a separate `const` at the top of the component.\n\nLet me also simplify the whole approach - move game loop to JS thread with requestAnimationFrame, avoid worklets entirely for web compatibility.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-czthl08wfsw3/src/components/game/GameCanvas.tsx]
Thought: Found it — there are two critical bugs:

1. **Rules of Hooks violation**: `useAnimatedStyle` called inside JSX (on the bomb-carry indicator) — this crashes the entire component silently
2. **`useFrameCallback` worklet** calling imported functions (`gameTick`, `COLLISION_RECTS`) that can't be safely accessed from the worklet context on web

Fixing both by moving to a plain `requestAnimationFrame` game loop + properly hoisted `useAnimatedStyle` hooks:
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
import React from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import Animated, {
  useSharedValue,
  useAnimatedStyle,
  useFrameCallback,
} from 'react-native-reanimated';

import {
  BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
  BOMB_SPAWN,
  PLAYER_SIZE,
  PLAYER_SPAWN,
} from '../../game/constants';
import { gameTick } from '../../game/gameLogic';
import type { GameState } from '../../game/types';
import { MAP_TILES } from '../../game/mapData';

interface GameCanvasProps {
  screenW: number;
  screenH: number;
  joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  isPaused: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<boolean>>;
  onFpsUpdate: (fps: number) => void;
  onTimerUpdate: (seconds: number) => void;
  onBombPickup: () => void;
  onGameOver: () => void;
}

const INITIAL_STATE: GameState = {
  player: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y,
    vx: 0,
    vy: 0,
    facing: 'right',
    animState: 'idle',
    animClock: 0,
    hasBomb: false,
  },
  camera: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x - 400,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y - 300,
    shakeIntensity: 0,
    shakeDuration: 0,
    shakeElapsed: 0,
  },
  bomb: {

    y: BOMB_SPAWN.y,
    pickedUp: false,
    countdown: BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
    exploded: false,
    explosionTime: 0,
  },

  isGameOver: false,
  fps: 60,
  fpsAccumulator: 0,
  fpsFrameCount: 0,
};

// Pre-render map tiles as static JSX (walls + crates)
const MAP_TILE_VIEWS = MAP_TILES.map((tile, i) => (
  <View
    key={i}
    style={[
      styles.tile,
      {
        left: tile.rect.x,
        top: tile.rect.y,
        width: tile.rect.w,
        height: tile.rect.h,
        backgroundColor: tile.type === 'wall' ? '#455a64' : '#795548',
        borderColor: tile.type === 'wall' ? '#37474f' : '#5d4037',
      },
    ]}
  />
));

export default function GameCanvas({
  screenW,
  screenH,
  joystickX,
  joystickY,
  isPaused,
  onFpsUpdate,
  onTimerUpdate,
  onBombPickup,
  onGameOver,
}: GameCanvasProps) {
  const gameState = useSharedValue<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);
  const elapsed   = useSharedValue(0);

  // World-space shared values — drive animated styles directly
  const camX     = useSharedValue(INITIAL_STATE.camera.x);
  const camY     = useSharedValue(INITIAL_STATE.camera.y);
  const shakeOffX = useSharedValue(0);
  const shakeOffY = useSharedValue(0);
  const playerX  = useSharedValue(PLAYER_SPAWN.x);
  const playerY  = useSharedValue(PLAYER_SPAWN.y);
  const bombX    = useSharedValue(BOMB_SPAWN.x);
  const bombY    = useSharedValue(BOMB_SPAWN.y);
  const bombPickedUp = useSharedValue(false);
  const bombExploded = useSharedValue(false);
  const hasBomb  = useSharedValue(false);

  // JS-thread mirror signals for HUD callbacks
  const fpsSignal      = useSharedValue(60);
  const timerSignal    = useSharedValue(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);
  const bombPickSignal = useSharedValue(false);
  const gameOverSignal = useSharedValue(false);

  // ── Main game loop — UI thread, ~60 fps ──────────────────────────────────────
  useFrameCallback((info) => {
    'worklet';
    const dtMs = info.timeSincePreviousFrame ?? 16.67;
    elapsed.value += dtMs / 1000;

    const state  = gameState.value;
    const merged = { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value };
    const next   = gameTick(merged, joystickX.value, joystickY.value, screenW, screenH, dtMs);
    gameState.value = next;

    // Update position shared values
    camX.value    = next.camera.x;
    camY.value    = next.camera.y;
    playerX.value = next.player.x;
    playerY.value = next.player.y;
    bombX.value   = next.bomb.x;
    bombY.value   = next.bomb.y;
    bombPickedUp.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    bombExploded.value = next.bomb.exploded;
    hasBomb.value  = next.player.hasBomb;

    // Camera shake offset
    shakeOffX.value = next.camera.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 47.3) * next.camera.shakeIntensity : 0;
    shakeOffY.value = next.camera.shakeIntensity > 0.5
      ? Math.sin(elapsed.value * 63.7) * next.camera.shakeIntensity : 0;

    // HUD signals
    fpsSignal.value      = next.fps;
    timerSignal.value    = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
    bombPickSignal.value = next.bomb.pickedUp;
    gameOverSignal.value = next.isGameOver;
  });

  // ── JS-thread polling: shared value signals → React state callbacks ──────────
  React.useEffect(() => {
    let rafId: number;
    let lastFps   = 60;
    let lastTimer = BOMB_COUNTDOWN;
    let lastPick  = false;
    let lastOver  = false;

    const poll = () => {
      const fps   = fpsSignal.value;
      const timer = timerSignal.value;
      const pick  = bombPickSignal.value;
      const over  = gameOverSignal.value;

      if (fps !== lastFps)    { lastFps  = fps;   onFpsUpdate(fps); }
      if (timer !== lastTimer){ lastTimer = timer; onTimerUpdate(timer); }
      if (pick && !lastPick)  { lastPick = true;   onBombPickup(); }
      if (over && !lastOver)  { lastOver = true;   onGameOver(); }

      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    };
    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(poll);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
  }, [fpsSignal, timerSignal, bombPickSignal, gameOverSignal,
      onFpsUpdate, onTimerUpdate, onBombPickup, onGameOver]);

  // ── Animated styles ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const worldStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    transform: [
      { translateX: -(camX.value + shakeOffX.value) },
      { translateY: -(camY.value + shakeOffY.value) },
    ],
  }));

  const playerStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left: playerX.value - PLAYER_SIZE / 2,
    top:  playerY.value - PLAYER_SIZE / 2,
  }));

  const bombStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left:    bombX.value - 15,
    top:     bombY.value - 15,
    opacity: bombPickedUp.value || bombExploded.value ? 0 : 1,
  }));

  const explosionStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left:    playerX.value - 80,
    top:     playerY.value - 80,
    opacity: bombExploded.value ? 1 : 0,
  }));

  return (
    <View style={[styles.viewport, { width: screenW, height: screenH }]}>
      {/* World container — translated by camera */}
      <Animated.View style={[styles.world, worldStyle]}>
        {/* Arena floor */}
        <View style={styles.floor} />

        {/* Static map tiles (walls + crates) */}
        {MAP_TILE_VIEWS}

        {/* Bomb (world-space, hidden when picked up) */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.bomb, bombStyle]}>
          <Text style={styles.bombEmoji}>💣</Text>
        </Animated.View>

        {/* Explosion flash */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.explosion, explosionStyle]} />

        {/* Player */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.player, playerStyle]}>
          <View style={styles.playerBody}>
            <Text style={styles.playerFace}>😎</Text>
          </View>
          {/* Bomb indicator above player when carrying */}
          <Animated.View style={useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
            opacity: hasBomb.value ? 1 : 0,
            position: 'absolute',
            top: -22,
            left: 5,
          }))}>
            <Text style={styles.carryBomb}>💣</Text>
          </Animated.View>
        </Animated.View>
      </Animated.View>
    </View>
  );
}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  viewport: {
    overflow: 'hidden',
    backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e',
  },
  world: {
    position: 'absolute',
    width: 1600,
    height: 1200,
  },
  floor: {
    position: 'absolute',
    left: 48,
    top: 48,
    width: 1504,
    height: 1104,
    backgroundColor: '#2d5a27',
```

```
import React, { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import Animated, {
  useSharedValue,
  useAnimatedStyle,
} from 'react-native-reanimated';

import {
  BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
  BOMB_SPAWN,
  PLAYER_SIZE,
  PLAYER_SPAWN,
} from '../../game/constants';
import { gameTick } from '../../game/gameLogic';
import type { GameState } from '../../game/types';
import { MAP_TILES } from '../../game/mapData';

interface GameCanvasProps {
  screenW: number;
  screenH: number;
  joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
  isPaused: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<boolean>>;
  onFpsUpdate: (fps: number) => void;
  onTimerUpdate: (seconds: number) => void;
  onBombPickup: () => void;
  onGameOver: () => void;
}

const INITIAL_STATE: GameState = {
  player: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y,
    vx: 0,
    vy: 0,
    facing: 'right',
    animState: 'idle',
    animClock: 0,
    hasBomb: false,
  },
  camera: {
    x: PLAYER_SPAWN.x - 400,
    y: PLAYER_SPAWN.y - 300,
    shakeIntensity: 0,
    shakeDuration: 0,
    shakeElapsed: 0,
  },
  bomb: {
    x: BOMB_SPAWN.x,
    y: BOMB_SPAWN.y,
    pickedUp: false,
    countdown: BOMB_COUNTDOWN,
    exploded: false,
    explosionTime: 0,
  },

    key={i}

      styles.tile,

        left: tile.rect.x,
        top: tile.rect.y,

export default function GameCanvas({
  screenW,
  screenH,
  joystickX,
  joystickY,
  isPaused,
  onFpsUpdate,
  onTimerUpdate,
  onBombPickup,
  onGameOver,
}: GameCanvasProps) {
  // Game state lives in a ref (mutated each frame, no re-render needed)
  const stateRef = useRef<GameState>(INITIAL_STATE);
  const lastTimeRef = useRef<number | null>(null);

  // Shared values that drive animated styles (updated from rAF loop on JS thread)
  const camX      = useSharedValue(INITIAL_STATE.camera.x);
  const camY      = useSharedValue(INITIAL_STATE.camera.y);
  const shakeOffX = useSharedValue(0);
  const shakeOffY = useSharedValue(0);
  const playerX   = useSharedValue(PLAYER_SPAWN.x);
  const playerY   = useSharedValue(PLAYER_SPAWN.y);
  const bombX     = useSharedValue(BOMB_SPAWN.x);
  const bombY     = useSharedValue(BOMB_SPAWN.y);
  const bombVisible  = useSharedValue(1);   // 1 = visible, 0 = hidden
  const explosionVis = useSharedValue(0);   // 0 = hidden, 1 = visible
  const hasBombVis   = useSharedValue(0);   // 0 = hidden, 1 = visible

  // ── Game loop via requestAnimationFrame (JS thread — works on all platforms) ──
  useEffect(() => {
    let rafId: number;
    // HUD callback de-bounce refs
    let lastTimer = BOMB_COUNTDOWN;
    let lastPick  = false;
    let lastOver  = false;
    let elapsedSec = 0;

    const tick = (now: number) => {
      const dtMs = lastTimeRef.current === null ? 16.67 : now - lastTimeRef.current;
      lastTimeRef.current = now;
      elapsedSec += dtMs / 1000;

      const state = stateRef.current;
      const next  = gameTick(
        { ...state, isPaused: isPaused.value },
        joystickX.value,
        joystickY.value,
        screenW,
        screenH,
        dtMs,
      );
      stateRef.current = next;

      // Update shared values → animated styles auto-update
      camX.value    = next.camera.x;
      camY.value    = next.camera.y;
      playerX.value = next.player.x;
      playerY.value = next.player.y;
      bombX.value   = next.bomb.x;
      bombY.value   = next.bomb.y;
      bombVisible.value  = next.bomb.pickedUp || next.bomb.exploded ? 0 : 1;
      explosionVis.value = next.bomb.exploded ? 1 : 0;
      hasBombVis.value   = next.player.hasBomb ? 1 : 0;

      // Camera shake offset
      shakeOffX.value = next.camera.shakeIntensity > 0.5
        ? Math.sin(elapsedSec * 47.3) * next.camera.shakeIntensity : 0;
      shakeOffY.value = next.camera.shakeIntensity > 0.5
        ? Math.sin(elapsedSec * 63.7) * next.camera.shakeIntensity : 0;

      // HUD callbacks (only when value changes)
      const timer = Math.ceil(next.bomb.countdown);
      if (timer !== lastTimer) { lastTimer = timer; onTimerUpdate(timer); }
      if (next.bomb.pickedUp && !lastPick) { lastPick = true; onBombPickup(); }
      if (next.isGameOver    && !lastOver) { lastOver = true; onGameOver(); }

      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    };

    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
  // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [screenW, screenH]);

  // ── Animated styles — all hooks must be at top level, never inside JSX ────────
  const worldStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    transform: [
      { translateX: -(camX.value + shakeOffX.value) },
      { translateY: -(camY.value + shakeOffY.value) },
    ],
  }));

  const playerStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left: playerX.value - PLAYER_SIZE / 2,
    top:  playerY.value - PLAYER_SIZE / 2,
  }));

  const bombStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left:    bombX.value - 15,
    top:     bombY.value - 15,
    opacity: bombVisible.value,
  }));

  const explosionStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    left:    playerX.value - 80,
    top:     playerY.value - 80,
    opacity: explosionVis.value,
  }));

  // ← fixed: hoisted out of JSX (was a hook-inside-JSX Rules of Hooks violation)
  const carryBombStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    opacity:  hasBombVis.value,
    position: 'absolute' as const,
    top:      -22,
    left:     5,
  }));

  return (
    <View style={[styles.viewport, { width: screenW, height: screenH }]}>
      {/* World container — translated by camera */}
      <Animated.View style={[styles.world, worldStyle]}>
        {/* Arena floor */}
        <View style={styles.floor} />

        {/* Static map tiles (walls + crates) */}
        {MAP_TILE_VIEWS}

        {/* Bomb (hidden when picked up or exploded) */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.bomb, bombStyle]}>
          <Text style={styles.bombEmoji}>💣</Text>
        </Animated.View>

        {/* Explosion flash */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.explosion, explosionStyle]} />

        {/* Player */}
        <Animated.View style={[styles.player, playerStyle]}>
          <View style={styles.playerBody}>
            <Text style={styles.playerFace}>😎</Text>
          </View>
          {/* Bomb carry indicator — style hoisted above, no hook inside JSX */}
          <Animated.View style={carryBombStyle}>
            <Text style={styles.carryBomb}>💣</Text>
          </Animated.View>
        </Animated.View>
      </Animated.View>
    </View>
  );
}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  viewport: {
    overflow: 'hidden',
    backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e',
```

     1 
     2 // AABB collision utilities — all functions are worklet-compatible
     3 
     4 import type { Rect } from './types';
     5 import { PLAYER_HALF } from './constants';
     6 
     7 /** Axis-Aligned Bounding Box overlap test */
     8 export function aabbOverlap(
     9   ax: number, ay: number, aw: number, ah: number,
    10   bx: number, by: number, bw: number, bh: number,
    11 ): boolean {
    12   return ax < bx + bw && ax + aw > bx && ay < by + bh && ay + ah > by;
    13 }
    14 
    15 /** Distance between two points */
    16 export function dist(ax: number, ay: number, bx: number, by: number): number {
    17   const dx = ax - bx;
    18   const dy = ay - by;
    19   return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    20 }
    21 
    22 /**
    23  * Resolve player AABB against all solid rects using separation vector.
    24  * Returns the corrected {px, py} after sliding collision.
    25  */
    26 export function resolveCollisions(
    27   px: number,
    28   py: number,
    29   collisionRects: Rect[],
    30 ): { px: number; py: number } {
    31   const hw = PLAYER_HALF;
    32   const hh = PLAYER_HALF;
    33 
    34   let cx = px;
    35   let cy = py;
    36 
    37   // Run 2 iterations for corner smoothing
    38   for (let iter = 0; iter < 2; iter++) {
    39     for (let i = 0; i < collisionRects.length; i++) {
    40       const r = collisionRects[i];
    41       if (!aabbOverlap(cx - hw, cy - hh, hw * 2, hh * 2, r.x, r.y, r.w, r.h)) {
    42         continue;
    43       }
    44       // Compute overlap on each axis
    45       const overlapLeft  = (cx + hw) - r.x;
    46       const overlapRight = (r.x + r.w) - (cx - hw);
    47       const overlapTop   = (cy + hh) - r.y;
    48       const overlapBot   = (r.y + r.h) - (cy - hh);
    49 
    50       // Push out along axis of minimum penetration
    51       const minX = Math.min(overlapLeft, overlapRight);
    52       const minY = Math.min(overlapTop, overlapBot);
    53 
    54       if (minX < minY) {
    55         if (overlapLeft < overlapRight) {
    56           cx -= overlapLeft;
    57         } else {
    58           cx += overlapRight;
    59         }
    60       } else {
    61         if (overlapTop < overlapBot) {
    62           cy -= overlapTop;
    63         } else {
    64           cy += overlapBot;
    65         }
    66       }
    67     }
    68   }
    69 
    70   return { px: cx, py: cy };
    71 }
    72 
    73 /** Clamp player position inside map bounds */
    74 export function clampToMap(
    75   px: number, py: number,
    76   mapW: number, mapH: number,
    77 ): { px: number; py: number } {
    78   return {
    79     px: Math.max(PLAYER_HALF, Math.min(mapW - PLAYER_HALF, px)),
    80     py: Math.max(PLAYER_HALF, Math.min(mapH - PLAYER_HALF, py)),
    81   };
    82 }

    12 export default function GameScreen() {

    14 
    15   // Joystick direction — shared values live on UI thread

    18

    21 
    22   // React state for HUD (updated from game loop via callbacks)
    23   const [fps, setFps] = useState(60);
    24   const [timerSeconds, setTimerSeconds] = useState(BOMB_COUNTDOWN);

    27   const [isGameOver, setIsGameOver] = useState(false);
    28

    30   const handleTimerUpdate = useCallback((v: number) => setTimerSeconds(v), []);
    31   const handleBombPickup = useCallback(() => setBombPickedUp(true), []);
    32   const handleGameOver = useCallback(() => setIsGameOver(true), []);
    33

    35     setIsPaused(true);

    38

     1 import React, { useCallback } from 'react';
     2 import { StyleSheet, View } from 'react-native';
     3 import { Gesture, GestureDetector } from 'react-native-gesture-handler';
     4 import Animated, {
     5   useAnimatedStyle,
     6   useSharedValue,
     7   runOnJS,
     8 } from 'react-native-reanimated';
     9 
    10 import {
    11   JOYSTICK_BASE_RADIUS,
    12   JOYSTICK_DEADZONE,
    13   JOYSTICK_KNOB_RADIUS,
    14 } from '../../game/constants';
    15 
    16 interface VirtualJoystickProps {
    17   joystickX: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
    18   joystickY: ReturnType<typeof useSharedValue<number>>;
    19 }
    20 
    21 const BASE = JOYSTICK_BASE_RADIUS;
    22 const KNOB = JOYSTICK_KNOB_RADIUS;
    23 const BASE_DIAM = BASE * 2;
    24 const KNOB_DIAM = KNOB * 2;
    25 
    26 export default function VirtualJoystick({ joystickX, joystickY }: VirtualJoystickProps) {
    27   const knobX = useSharedValue(0);
    28   const knobY = useSharedValue(0);
    29   const active = useSharedValue(false);
    30 
    31   const panGesture = Gesture.Pan()
    32     .onBegin(() => {
    33       'worklet';
    34       active.value = true;
    35     })
    36     .onUpdate((e) => {
    37       'worklet';
    38       const dx = e.translationX;
    39       const dy = e.translationY;
    40       const len = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    41       const maxLen = BASE - KNOB;
    42 
    43       if (len > 0) {
    44         const clampLen = Math.min(len, maxLen);
    45         const nx = dx / len;
    46         const ny = dy / len;
    47         knobX.value = nx * clampLen;
    48         knobY.value = ny * clampLen;
    49 
    50         // Normalise to -1..1 with deadzone
    51         const inputLen = clampLen / maxLen;
    52         if (inputLen > JOYSTICK_DEADZONE) {
    53           joystickX.value = nx;
    54           joystickY.value = ny;
    55         } else {
    56           joystickX.value = 0;
    57           joystickY.value = 0;
    58         }
    59       }
    60     })
    61     .onEnd(() => {
    62       'worklet';
    63       active.value = false;
    64       knobX.value = 0;
    65       knobY.value = 0;
    66       joystickX.value = 0;
    67       joystickY.value = 0;
    68     })
    69     .onFinalize(() => {
    70       'worklet';
    71       active.value = false;
    72       knobX.value = 0;
    73       knobY.value = 0;
    74       joystickX.value = 0;
    75       joystickY.value = 0;
    76     });
    77 
    78   const knobStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    79     transform: [
    80       { translateX: knobX.value },
    81       { translateY: knobY.value },
    82     ],
    83   }));
    84 
    85   const baseStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    86     opacity: active.value ? 0.85 : 0.65,
    87   }));
    88 
    89   return (
    90     <GestureDetector gesture={panGesture}>
    91       <Animated.View style={[styles.base, baseStyle]}>
    92         {/* Outer ring decorations */}
    93         <View style={styles.ring} />
    94         {/* Direction dots */}
    95         {[0, 90, 180, 270].map((deg) => (
    96           <View
    97             key={deg}
    98             style={[
    99               styles.dirDot,
   100               {
   101                 transform: [
   102                   { rotate: `${deg}deg` },
   103                   { translateY: -(BASE - 12) },
   104                 ],
   105               },
   106             ]}
   107           />
   108         ))}
   109         {/* Knob */}
   110         <Animated.View style={[styles.knob, knobStyle]} />
   111       </Animated.View>
   112     </GestureDetector>
   113   );
   114 }
   115 
   116 const styles = StyleSheet.create({
   117   base: {
   118     width: BASE_DIAM,
   119     height: BASE_DIAM,
   120     borderRadius: BASE,
   121     backgroundColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)',
   122     borderWidth: 3,
   123     borderColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.45)',
   124     alignItems: 'center',
   125     justifyContent: 'center',
   126   },
   127   ring: {
   128     position: 'absolute',
   129     width: BASE_DIAM - 20,
   130     height: BASE_DIAM - 20,
   131     borderRadius: BASE - 10,
   132     borderWidth: 1.5,
   133     borderColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)',
   134   },
   135   dirDot: {
   136     position: 'absolute',
   137     width: 6,
   138     height: 6,
   139     borderRadius: 3,
   140     backgroundColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)',
   141   },
   142   knob: {
   143     width: KNOB_DIAM,
   144     height: KNOB_DIAM,
   145     borderRadius: KNOB,
   146     backgroundColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.85)',
   147     borderWidth: 2.5,
   148     borderColor: 'rgba(200,200,255,0.6)',
   149     shadowColor: '#000',
   150     shadowOffset: { width: 0, height: 2 },
   151     shadowOpacity: 0.3,
   152     shadowRadius: 4,
   153     elevation: 4,
   154   },
   155 });
   156

    13 interface GameUIProps {

    23 export default function GameUI({
    24   fps,

    26   bombPickedUp,
    27   isPaused,
    28   isGameOver,
    29   onPause,
    30   onResume,
    31 }: GameUIProps) {
    32   const urgent = bombPickedUp && timerSeconds <= 5;
    33   const timerColor = urgent ? '#FF3333' : timerSeconds <= 10 ? '#FF9933' : '#FFFFFF';
    34

    50               </Text>

    68           </Pressable>
    69         </View>
    70       </View>

    73       {isPaused && !isGameOver && (

    79           <View style={styles.pauseCard}>

    87

There are multiple issues:\n\n1. **GameUI.tsx uses `FadeIn`, `FadeOut` from Reanimated** - these entering/exiting animations may crash on web if Reanimated isn't properly set up.\n\n2. **VirtualJoystick.tsx uses `GestureDetector` from react-native-gesture-handler** - this requires the gesture handler to be initialized properly.\n\n3. **The viewport sizing issue** - `GameCanvas` uses `{width: screenW, height: screenH}` and if `screenW=0` initially, nothing shows.\n\nThe CORE problem is that `react-native-reanimated` and `react-native-gesture-handler` may not be initializing properly on web in this preview environment.\n\n**The definitive fix**: Complete rewrite using ZERO external animation/gesture libraries.
